Germany does not want to participate in the Disarmament Conference until Europe grants it the right to equality in armaments, but France is determined not to recognize this right.

Reuters, Geneva, 15th – France's proposal to reduce armaments and ensure security, which has now been submitted to the core leadership of the Disarmament Conference, has aroused considerable goodwill. However, according to general criticism, the French plan is extremely complex. The US representative here [is critical of] an article recently published in the Japan Diplomatic Times by Mr. Tamaki Hanzawa, entitled "Re-addressing the Chinese People," in which the Northeast Incident is entirely blamed on China, while the author completely absolves himself of any responsibility, and attempts to lure the Chinese people with direct negotiations. The intentions and wording are extremely flawed. This newspaper has already written a rebuttal in its commentary column and translated the original text of Hanzawa here so that readers can understand the deceptive tactics of the Japanese, who will stop at nothing.

Since the Shanghai Incident, Chinese compatriots seem to have realized that the anti-Japanese policy is not feasible. They seem to have experienced that relying solely on the League of Nations or the forces of third countries like the United States to put pressure on Japan has completely failed. At the same time, they are deeply aware that if they want a final resolution, they must base it on direct negotiations between China and Japan. We have given extremely earnest advice to the Chinese government and the Chinese people. The main points of this advice are: First, China should first withdraw its petition to the League regarding the Manchuria issue. Second, China should quickly establish a strong and lasting government capable of taking on the important task of direct negotiations between China and Japan. If China can truly implement these two conditions, then we would not hesitate to carefully consider the issue of Manchuria's suzerainty, which Chinese compatriots have lamented and considered the most important issue. This advice seems to have won some reaction from Chinese public opinion and has prompted considerable consideration by many informed people. As a result, the Chinese government's actual policies have violated our advice. Not only has it not withdrawn its petition to the League, but it has also newly appointed Gu Weijun as the plenipotentiary representative to the League and promoted various anti-Japanese policies. The policy of relying on the League directly and indirectly against Japan remains unchanged.

2. What will be the development of the situation as a result of this? In Japan, the recognition of Manchukuo has officially worsened the perception of China in the world. Not only that, but after the publication of the Lytton Report, the reality of China was exposed, which aroused a negative reaction from world public opinion toward China. The past sympathy for China has become a fleeting bubble. Shouldn't the Chinese people reflect on these facts?

However, how are these established facts unfolding? Now, let's first talk about Japan's recognition of Manchuria. Japan's recognition of Manchukuo is indeed a difficult issue for China. China's diplomacy is indeed in a deadlock because of Japan's recognition of Manchukuo. But this is definitely not Japan's intention to make things difficult for China, to put China's diplomacy in a deadlock. This is truly a sincere appeal, hoping that China can withdraw its petition to the League and declare its sincerity in direct negotiations between China and Japan, and not trap itself in difficulties or deadlocks. At the same time, before the recognition of Manchukuo, Japan did have a very clear attitude. At that time, as long as the other party had the sincerity to accept this proposal, (Japan would strongly advocate direct negotiations between China and Japan in the League). However, the Chinese government not only did not accept our earnest advice, but instead acted in reverse. As a result, Japan resolutely recognized Manchukuo. If we use the style of the Spring and Autumn Annals, we can say, "China's anti-Japanese policy and League dependence ultimately led Japan to recognize Manchukuo."

3. To make it easier for the Chinese people to understand, let us further explain the significance of the recognition of Manchukuo. As a result of Japan's recognition of Manchukuo, Manchuria has neither become Japanese territory nor a Japanese colony. On the contrary, Manchukuo can have independent sovereignty because of Japan's recognition. Manchukuo has obtained equal authority that does not take Japan's freedom as its own. Therefore, just for the convenience of Japan, rather than recognizing Manchukuo with equal sovereignty and increasing future worries, it would be more beneficial to sign a strict treaty with China to determine the nature of Manchuria. For example, the Kwantung Leased Territory has always been a region legally entrusted under Chinese sovereignty, but according to the Sino-Japanese Treaty, Japan already had lease rights, which amounted to almost complete control. What is the use of such paper sovereignty? When determining the nature of Manchuria, we no longer considered sovereignty to be a major issue, let alone suzerainty. However, has the Chinese government not considered these issues? Has it not been given the opportunity to comment on this issue? Isn't this a good proof that China has not withdrawn its petition to the League and has not declared its sincerity in direct negotiations between China and Japan? Therefore, from Japan's point of view, it cannot but believe that the Chinese government has abandoned Manchuria's sovereignty, suzerainty, and all rights to speak. The Chinese people must remember this fact.

4. Therefore, in fact, Manchuria is a masterless region. Japan can occupy it or even annex it. However, Japan has repeatedly declared to the world that Japan has no ambition for Manchuria. Of course, Japan does not want to directly rule Manchuria, nor does it want Manchuria to rely on China or the League of Nations. It has no choice but to tolerate the local independence movement. Recently, it has officially recognized the Manchukuo government. The governance of Manchuria can only rely on the talents of the residents of Manchuria. All of these are the aims of Japanese policy. In other words, Japan had to recognize the independence of Manchuria in order to avoid the suspicion of annexing Manchuria. This can be seen from the fact that Japan spent more than half a year just on the issue of recognition. During this period, it gave China ample opportunity to consider and gave China the time to study the best means. However, the Chinese government did not forgive Japan's true intentions and did not accept our advice, which ultimately determined the status of Manchuria today.

Therefore, the emergence of Manchukuo was not something that Japan took from China, but something that China itself abandoned. Because China itself did not exercise its right to speak, as a result, Manchukuo became independent and Japan recognized it. If there are Chinese people who hold different views on this accomplished fact, then let me tell you, rather than resenting Japan, you should blame your own government for not being good, and rather than blaming your own government, you should reflect on the failure of the anti-Japanese policy and the League-dependent policy. All of these are for the Chinese people to reflect on the issue of Manchukuo.

5. Next, let's talk about the relationship between the League of Nations and China. Since last year, China has regarded the League of Nations as its only savior, believing that crying to the League of Nations would definitely buy the sympathy of the League. But what is the situation today? Let's first discuss the Lytton Report that the Chinese government and public have been looking forward to. Of course, Japan will severely criticize this report. But is the report unconditionally beneficial to China? Wise Chinese compatriots should reflect on this. If China relies on this report and the League of Nations' awareness of China as shown in this report, how will China be dominated by the League in the future?

First, on the Manchuria issue, although Chinese compatriots have been clamoring to restore lost territory, pleading for the sympathy of the League's investigative countries, and eagerly hoping for the return of Manchuria, the Lytton Report has made it clear that "it is no longer possible to restore the situation before September of last year." At the same time, it advocates establishing a "broad" system of "autonomy." In this autonomous government, in addition to the condition that Japanese occupy a sufficient proportion, although the other contents are not very clear, on the other hand, it believes that any solution that does not consider the historical relationship between Japan and Manchuria will be invalid. At the same time, it advocates using an effective constabulary to maintain internal order in Manchuria. From these points of view, Manchuria's autonomy is an autonomy based on Japan's existing power. The so-called constabulary naturally refers to the current Japanese garrison in Manchuria. If that is the case, then the difference between Japan's independent recognition and the Lytton Report's Manchuria settlement plan is only a slight one. The only difference here is whether the League of Nations can seize the opportunity to intervene in Manchuria. At the same time, the investigation team's fundamental understanding of Manchuria is based on the fact that the sources of administration of mainland China and Manchuria must be separated. Therefore, the investigation team has given a judgment of "impossible" to China's so-called restoration of lost territory. Here, are the Chinese people still expecting the League to resolve the Manchuria issue?

6. The second is the issue of China itself. According to the predictions of the Lytton Report, it has already constituted the premise of China's international management. The articles in the report are written by outstanding diplomats. Naturally, the description is very clever and tactful. However, according to the investigation team's "view of China," China's political instability and the obstacles to Sino-Japanese relations are all cancers of peace in the Far East and fears of world peace. These "instabilities" are all due to China's lack of a strong central government. Therefore, in order to implement China's internal transformation, there must be temporary international cooperation. The so-called international cooperation is naturally international management. Although the report does not explain its method, it is clear that the purpose of the report is to say that China's internal strife, political disputes, and socio-economic instability will inevitably affect the instability of countries related to China, giving the peace of the world a heavy threat, so it must be resolved by international cooperation. The significance of China's expectations for the League of Nations' investigation team is obscured. The investigation team that China originally wanted to rely on as a lawyer has instead become a judge and ruled that China is guilty. Then, does China want to expose its dark side to the world and arouse the heavy pressure of international forces before inviting the investigation team to sue Japan? Or does China want to resist Japan on the one hand and willingly accept the heavy pressure of European and American countries on the other? Wise Chinese compatriots should calmly consider this proposal at this time.

7. There are many things about the Lytton Report that China should reflect on and savor. The most important thing to pay attention to here is of course the key point of the Manchuria autonomy plan and the China international management plan. Then, what is the atmosphere of the League of Nations itself? Recently, there has been a very great change. If the phrase "League atmosphere" has meaning, then we can say that the internal and external leading countries of the League, Britain, France, Italy, Germany, and even the United States, have changed their public opinion trends on the Manchuria issue. "Japan is invading China, and China is an organized civilized country." Originally, the tension of the League of Nations started from these false premises. Now, European and American countries have abandoned this premise and are completely observing the Sino-Japanese issue from a new understanding. As a result, like the Lytton Report, European and American governments and public opinion have understood the particularity of the Far East and no longer lightly make judgments based on Western European international common sense. The problem that is now troubling the heads of the great powers in the League is the urgent problems of Europe itself, the problem of the League's own survival. In other words, before these problems, the Manchuria issue is a very small problem. If the League has to consider whether to lose Japan or China for the sake of the Manchuria issue, of course it will not lose Japan for the sake of China. Therefore, at future League meetings, we think it is unlikely that the League of Nations will destroy itself by breaking up the League itself because of China. Recently, public opinion in various countries has turned to a compromise pro-Japanese position. Even Sterling of the United States cannot but remain silent before these opinions. Aren't these the first issues that the Chinese people should seriously reflect on?

8. However, Chinese compatriots, are you still expecting the League of Nations now? Are you still planning to call the League of Nations the savior of China and entrust your fate to it? If China can truly rely on the League of Nations to open up its national destiny, Japan's interests may be sacrificed, and it will not be a pity to let go of Manchuria. However, the meaning of the League has already been revealed in the Lytton Report. The real meaning is China's international management and the white man's conquest of Asia. They are hoping for the Sino-Japanese conflict to sharpen their claws for plundering the Far East. This is like the three-nation intervention after the Sino-Japanese War and the lease of the Far East after the three-nation intervention. At the same time, it is also like the politicians of the Beiyang faction who induced the forces of the powers and opened the beginning of the partitioning of China. Now, the Kuomintang government's wrong League-dependent policy has opened the beginning of China's international management. These are all very obvious facts. Chinese compatriots, are you not indignant at the current situation?

Originally, Europeans and Americans are not very clear about the international politics of the East and the national psychology of the East. Therefore, Japan's consistent policy is not to allow Europe and the United States to interfere in the issues of East Asia. Therefore, Sino-Japanese disputes should be resolved based on direct Sino-Japanese negotiations. Japan itself not only did not file a complaint to the League of Nations, but also always hid China's shortcomings and shattered the plans of various countries for China whenever there was an opportunity (such as the Chinese railway management plan waiting for the Lincheng Incident) to protect China's independent sovereignty. This time, the Sino-Japanese issue was brought to the League of Nations, and the League's judgment was based on the premise of China's international management. This was completely expected. Therefore, Japan did not want to hope for the League's judgment on last year's sudden incident. Whenever China roared in the League, Japan always advocated direct Sino-Japanese negotiations and always hoped for a satisfactory resolution of the situation. However, the Chinese government used the League of Nations' lack of understanding of East Asian affairs as a rare commodity to live in, strongly slandering Japan and strongly inviting the League's intervention. As a result, it not only brought about today's accomplished facts and constituted the premise of international management, but also this issue is really related to the overall situation of East Asia and the fate of the entire East Asian nation, and it is not just a Manchuria issue. Therefore, wise Chinese compatriots must first overthrow this government and secondly, sweep away the government and traitorous politicians who brought about the demise of the country and renew the national policy. (Translated by Sun Huaiyu)

Progress of the Anti-Japanese Army in Rehe

Overall Rectification of Embankment Affairs in Hubei Province by the Headquarters

Concerning the Water Conservancy Bureau and the Embankment Works Bureau, and the Funds Custody Committee.

Original Projects Transferred to the National Economic Committee for Handling

A Water Conservancy and Embankment Works Clearance Committee is formed to conclude outstanding cases.

Hankou Correspondence: The Commander-in-Chief Headquarters of the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces, concerned with the haphazard construction of embankments in Hubei Province and the embezzlement by officials, leading to last year's unprecedented floods, finds a thorough rectification necessary to eliminate chronic problems. On the 15th, the Hubei Provincial Government was ordered to abolish the Water Conservancy Bureau, the Embankment Works Bureau, and the Embankment Works Funds Custody Committee. All water conservancy and embankment works affairs are to be transferred to the National Economic Committee for overall management, and a letter was sent for verification. The original embankment works funds will continue to be collected as before. A new Custody Committee will be formed to be responsible for safekeeping, preventing misappropriation. The Headquarters will organize a Hubei Embankment Works Affairs Clearance Committee to clear outstanding cases. The regulations of the above two committees will be formulated and promulgated simultaneously, marking a major reform in Hubei's water conservancy and embankment works. The original order is recorded as follows (details of the regulations omitted):

Order to the Hubei Provincial Government: Water conservancy and embankments are crucial to the livelihood of the people, safeguarding farmland and facilitating irrigation and transportation. Therefore, officials are appointed to manage these affairs, bearing a significant responsibility. However, the floods this year caused devastation, with embankments along the Yangtze and Han rivers collapsing one after another, resulting in widespread inundation. People and livestock perished, and property was destroyed, marking a calamity unseen in a century. The root cause lies in the Hubei Provincial Government's negligence in construction affairs over the years, failing to implement comprehensive planning, adopting simplistic solutions, and neglecting oversight. There was a lack of preparation beforehand, and hasty action afterward, wasting national resources and causing a catastrophe. Thinking of this, we feel deep sorrow. The Hubei embankment funds receive a substantial amount of revenue each year, yet management is so careless, allowing officials to arbitrarily embezzle funds.

Corruption is rampant, and there is no regard for the lives and property of the people. Such greed is intolerable. A thorough reorganization is necessary to rectify the situation and prevent future disasters. Moreover, rivers and waterways generally span thousands of miles, traversing numerous provinces and counties. Comprehensive planning is essential to ensure overall prosperity. If regions are divided, it will be difficult to achieve perfection. Therefore, after last year's major disaster, the National Government's Flood Relief Committee developed an overall plan for embankment construction, benefiting various provinces, as evidenced by the facts. It is now verified that the embankment works constructed by the Flood Relief Committee have been transferred to the National Economic Committee. The Committee has the Jianghan Engineering Bureau in Hankou, which manages the Yangtze River embankments from Huangmei County to Tuomaobu in Jianli, and the Han River from Hankou to Shayang. All projects in the province fall within its jurisdiction. The province need not establish separate embankment works and water conservancy agencies, which only create redundancy. All projects can be integrated and managed by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau. The original Hubei Embankment Works Funds Custody Committee, Hubei Provincial Embankment Works Bureau, and Hubei Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau, etc., are to be abolished to reduce redundancy and conserve resources. The various projects originally handled by the Water Conservancy Bureau and the Embankment Works Bureau should be transferred to the National Economic Committee for overall planning and management, and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau should be responsible for managing them nearby. The original designated embankment works funds, such as the surcharges on customs duties, special taxes, and land taxes, should continue to be collected as before. A separate Custody Committee for special embankment funds should be formed to ensure that the funds are used exclusively for embankment works and water conservancy projects in the province, preventing unauthorized use, and ensuring proper auditing. The previous outstanding cases and various documents of the agencies should be handled by a Hubei Water Conservancy and Embankment Works Affairs Clearance Committee organized by the Headquarters.

Letter to the National Economic Committee: Water conservancy in Hubei is of great importance, and the collection of special embankment funds is intended for timely repairs to benefit the people. However, due to mismanagement over the years, corruption has been rampant, resulting in the squandering of funds and frequent floods. All embankment and water conservancy affairs in the province should be fundamentally reformed to eliminate chronic problems and conserve resources. Furthermore, water conservancy involves several provinces, and if each locality divides its own territory, it will be difficult to achieve overall success. Comprehensive planning is essential to centralize authority. The Hubei Water Conservancy Bureau, Hubei Provincial Embankment Works Bureau, and Hubei Embankment Works Funds Custody Committee are hereby abolished. All original embankment and water conservancy projects are to be transferred to your Committee for management and planning. All necessary projects and affairs should be undertaken by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau in Hankou. The original embankment funds, including the surcharges on customs duties, special taxes, and land taxes, should continue to be collected as before. A separate Custody Committee should be formed to be responsible for safekeeping, ensuring that all funds are used for embankment and water conservancy projects in the province and not diverted for other purposes. Regarding the outstanding cases and disputes related to the abolished bureaus and committees, the Headquarters will organize a Hubei Embankment Works Affairs Clearance Committee to conduct a thorough investigation and ensure closure. (November 15th)

Hunan Province Holds Anti-Smoking Publicity Week

▲ Anti-Smoking Parade with 50,000 to 60,000 People

▲ Burning of Opium and Parading of Opium Offenders Through the Streets

Changsha Correspondence: To demonstrate its determination to ban opium, the Hunan Provincial Government has established an Anti-Smoking Committee, with He Jian as the chairman. Leaders from the Party, government, and military have been appointed as committee members to oversee all matters. The 34th Division under Chen Quzhen, which previously used special opium seedling taxes for military expenses, has been ordered to immediately cease registering opium seedlings. The provincial treasury will allocate 20,000 yuan per month starting from November to compensate for the loss. Meanwhile, Party, government, and military organizations, along with civic groups, have jointly organized the "Hunan People's Anti-Smoking Publicity Week General Assembly Preparatory Office." A street parade will be held at the Provincial Education Association grounds at 9:00 AM today (the 14th) to expand anti-smoking publicity. Approximately 50,000 to 60,000 people from all walks of life are expected to attend. All public and private schools in the provincial capital will be closed for the day to allow full participation. He Jian will preside over the assembly. After the ceremony, He Jian will report on the significance of the meeting, followed by speeches from Xie Zuyiao and Tan Changkai, members of the Provincial Party Committee. The main points can be summarized as follows: (1) Banning opium is essential to save the declining Chinese nation and preserve China's international reputation. (2) To ban opium, it is necessary to simultaneously prohibit cultivation, transportation, sale, and consumption. (3) To ban opium, the government and the people must work together. After the speeches, the assembly unanimously decided to elect ten representatives, including Quan Shi, Tan Huang, Yun Tang, Gan Chen, and Jie Shi, to petition the Party and government organs in writing. The petition calls for the immediate abolition of the special tax collection agency and the execution of opium offenders to demonstrate the government's and the people's unified determination to reject drugs. A telegram will also be sent to urge the entire country to strictly enforce the opium ban. At that time, Peng Changzhuo, chief of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, will bring 5,249 pieces of opium paraphernalia, 200.06 taels of raw opium, 254.06 taels of opium paste, 220 taels of opium residue, 56 taels of opium ash, five opium lamps, and thirty-six opium offenders, including Liu Qingxiang, who have been seized in recent days, to the assembly grounds. The opium paraphernalia, paste, etc., will be burned on the spot, and the opium offenders will be paraded through the streets. When the opium is burned, the procession will immediately depart, with automobiles leading the way and the opium offenders at the rear. The parade will proceed from the Provincial Education Association, through Shuifengjing, Xuegong Street, Beizheng Street, Yuanmen, Shangfu Zheng Street, Bajiaoting, Pozi Street, Taipingmen, Fuxingmen, and into Zhongshan West Road, before returning to the Provincial Education Association and dispersing. Along the way, slogans such as "Execute Opium Offenders" and "People Voluntarily Report Opium Offenders" will be chanted. Crowds of onlookers will line the streets. After the meeting, ten automobiles will be dispatched to various parts of Changsha City to distribute leaflets with the message "Admonishing Opium Addicts Not to Enter a Dead End." The opium offenders will be divided into four districts (east, south, west, and north), with ten soldiers escorting nine offenders in each district, and paraded through the streets of Changsha City. Two airplanes will also be dispatched to fly over the city and suburbs to distribute anti-smoking leaflets. From 2:00 PM onwards, publicity teams will simultaneously depart to publicize the necessity of banning opium. (The entire city is divided into 113 districts, with a publicity team assigned to each district. Each team, consisting of five to ten people, is formed by schools, government agencies, organizations, and Party branches at all levels. The publicity campaign will run from the 14th to the 20th, with on-site publicity from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM each afternoon.) Anti-smoking publicity teams will deliver speeches in public at every street corner and alleyway. At 2:30 PM, the petition representatives, Quan Shi, and others, will first go to the Provincial Government to personally deliver the petition, requesting the abolition of the special tax agency and the execution of opium offenders. He Jian will respond, fully accepting the second point, while stating that the special tax agency is under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance and promising to immediately telegraph the Ministry for consultation. Subsequently, the representatives will go to the Provincial Party Committee to petition. Zhu Haohuai, a committee member, will receive them and promise to promptly forward the two points of the petition to the government for action. Judging from today's situation, the atmosphere for banning opium in Hunan Province is indeed very tense. It is hoped that the authorities and the people will persevere and not slacken their efforts in the future. (November 14th)

Local Correspondence Songjiang

Bran Cake Industry Protests Business Tax The Bran Cake Trade Association of Fengjing Town in this county telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that the business tax on the bran cake industry, as stipulated this time, is collected at a rate of 0.5%, which is more than four times higher than last year. It has been observed that the area along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway has suffered repeated military disasters and floods in recent years, and the people are impoverished to the extreme. This year, silk cocoons have plummeted in price, and rice prices have fallen sharply, and the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. Bran cake is used by rural people for raising livestock and fertilizing fields. Although the business tax is directly levied on merchants, it is indirectly taken from farmers. Imposing a heavy burden on the impoverished people will likely lead to desperation and affect public security. Moreover, during the lijin era, bran cake was never taxed. Even the business tax regulations do not explicitly stipulate taxation on bran cake. When the business tax was first implemented last year, the trade association, deeply aware of the country's financial difficulties, agreed to pay 0.1% for retail and 0.05% for wholesale, simply to endure the pain for the sake of the overall situation. Now, the tax rate has been increased drastically, which the people cannot bear. In recent years, fertilizer powder has been selling well in the market. Our country's native fertilizer materials have been encroached upon year after year, leaving them with almost no foothold. If domestic fertilizers are not supported and instead have their taxes increased, it is tantamount to suppressing domestic goods and promoting foreign goods. We implore you to investigate the situation and refrain from increasing the business tax on the bran cake industry, maintaining the original tax rate. We await your instructions with utmost urgency.

Wuxi

Police Arrest Armed Robbers Shi Shaoqing, a police officer at the Wuqiao Substation outside the North Gate, received a report from Zhang Guiqing and Li Zhenxiang that a man from Anhui named Dun Sen was carrying a weapon and intending to commit robbery at the dock of a certain shipping company under Wuqiao. The police officer sounded the alarm and took the reporters to the police station, then together with the patrol leader went to arrest Guo. A Browning pistol and four bullets were found on him. He was immediately sent to the Fifth Sub-bureau for interrogation. Tragic News of the Suicide of the Manager of Sanmao The manager of Sanmao Southern Goods Store on Nanchang Street outside the South Gate, Qiang Bingxiang, was known for his loyalty, honesty, and frugality, and was deeply trusted by the store owner. Bingxiang had a younger brother named Juquan, who used to be a partner in Shengsheng Paper Store in the north. Because of losses from small deals, he owed more than 500 yuan, leading to the store's closure. Creditors pressed hard, so Bingxiang acted as guarantor. Last winter, because of his younger sister's marriage, Bingxiang alone paid for the expenses, causing a loss of more than 1,000 yuan to the store. Moreover, his wife was addicted to gambling, leading to accumulating debts and an increasingly difficult situation. The morning before, Bingxiang had an argument with his wife over financial issues. After the argument, his wife ran out in a fit of anger, jumping into the river nearby, intending to commit suicide. Fortunately, she was rescued by passersby and did not drown. Bingxiang saw his wife crying and his children wailing, and feeling overwhelmed by grief at the state of his family, he developed a desire to end his life. So, yesterday morning, he secretly took arsenic and committed suicide. After taking the poison, he still went to Sanmao and sat in the store, secretly crying. About an hour later, he felt excruciating pain in his abdomen, followed by bleeding from all seven orifices. The shop assistants were shocked and immediately sent him to Puren Hospital, but it was too late to save him, and he died. Afterward, his elderly parents cried bitterly, almost passing out from grief, which was truly tragic.

Chamber of Commerce Discusses Business Volume Regarding the declaration of business volume for business tax purposes, the Chamber of Commerce has held repeated consultations, but the declared amount is still short by 2 million yuan. In the recent meeting, apart from a small number of merchants who slightly increased their declared volume, the rest either did not attend or did not increase their volume, resulting in no result. The Chamber's Executive Committee reported that they will continue to encourage various industries to try their best to increase the declared volume, while also requesting the authorities to appropriately reduce the target to avoid failure. Unexpectedly, before the Chamber could give its final reply, the Tax Bureau began investigating the accounts of various businesses. The businesses being investigated, such as Hu Dade Tai, requested the Chamber to negotiate for a postponement. The Tax Bureau agreed to send the investigated figures to the Chamber for reference and to temporarily refrain from taking administrative actions. The accounts have been sent to the Chamber, and the investigation results show that most of them do not match. The Tax Bureau is even more assertive, demanding that the Chamber make a final decision promptly. Otherwise, it will continue to investigate the accounts and, at the same time, follow the Provincial Department's order to collect taxes on all businesses that engage in both wholesale and retail, based on the retail tax rate. The Chamber then convened another meeting with various industries yesterday to decide to increase the original declared volume by 10%.

Ministry of Finance Approves Price Increase for Official Salt The salt produced by various salt production companies in Lianghuai Jinan Field is mostly sold to the four banks of Hubei, Hunan, Western Anhui, and Western Hunan. The salt price was verified and stipulated by the government in the third year of the Republic based on the cost situation at that time. By the 15th and 16th years of the Republic, the cost of various expenses under the company such as the stove grain shop, contract labor, handling charges, barge freight and ferry fees had increased with the level of social life. The company applied for a price increase, which was approved by the Ministry of Finance after repeated consideration. The price increase for each stone in Hubei and Hunan banks is 2.5 cents, the price increase for each stone in Western Huai is 1.5 cents, and the price increase for each stone in Anhui bank is 2 cents.

Free Talk

Two One-Branch Talks

Returning from Siam

— Zhan Lu

Those who pay attention to the world situation all know the situation in Siam after the coup this year, because Siam not only belongs to the same race and continent as our country, but also became a republic from autocracy.

The Siamese people migrated south from the Pamir Plateau and are of the same race as our country. The history promulgated by the Ministry of Education of Siam says this: the ancestral home of the Siamese people was in China, but they were deceived by the Tang people to move south. It can be seen that the Siamese people have already recognized that they are a branch of the Chinese nation.

This time, the Southwest Political Council and the Guangdong Provincial Government sent Lin Yizhong to congratulate the Siamese government on the success of the revolution and to investigate the situation in Siam after the coup; he has now returned to Guangdong to report on the general situation during the Joint Commemoration Week.

According to Mr. Lin, China and Siam are not treaty countries, and the Siamese government has never received Chinese figures with political color; but this time it was different, and they were treated with national courtesy and were extremely grand; it can be seen that the Siamese government after the coup has improved its treatment of China. Moreover, the current deputy commanders of various armies and ministers of various departments are all descendants of overseas Chinese. For example, the sons-in-law of Mr. Xiao Fucheng are all holding important positions in the Siamese government; the speaker of the Senate, Mr. So-and-So, said that his family still keeps the "Guanglu Dafu" title plaque from China, and the Minister of Foreign Affairs is also from Wenchang County, China. The total population of Siam is 10 million, and overseas Chinese account for one-fifth; among them, Chaozhou people are the most numerous, followed by Fuzhou people. Siamese customs and habits are like a second Chaozhou, and it is really impossible to distinguish between Chinese and Siamese people; because overseas Chinese in Siam can serve as officials as soon as they pay the import tax; now the governors of various provinces in Siam are all filled by Chaozhou and Fuzhou people, etc.

Alas! Since the fall of Guandong, everyone has a feeling of "I look around, but there is nowhere to go;" but unexpectedly, within Siam, overseas Chinese still occupy so much power; after reading Mr. Lin's speech, everyone deserves to smile through tears. I especially introduce it to the general readers in order to encourage the spirit of our people to develop abroad.

Relics from the January 28th Battle

— Zou Tianma

丨Exhibition at Jinan University丨

During the January 28th Incident last year, Zhabei became a war zone. The National Jinan University was first the headquarters of the 19th Route Army, and then a front-line hospital for the Red Cross. After the 19th Route Army retreated, it was occupied by the Japanese army. The school suffered terrible devastation, and all the school equipment and specimens were destroyed. Our country's institutions of higher education have become enemy barracks, which is truly regrettable.

After the Japanese army withdrew, fortunately, the school's administrators worked hard, and within a few months, it gradually returned to its former appearance. Moreover, starting from this semester, the school is running its own power plant and printing house, and is also rigorously training students. This is not necessarily a good phenomenon in our country's education.

On the 11th and 12th of this month, the school held a chrysanthemum exhibition. On this occasion, the items left by the Japanese army in the school were also displayed. I once went to see it, and there were many clogs, stationery, stretchers, and miscellaneous items. There was also a shell of a bomb dropped from the air, and a set of Japanese monk's clothing. What deserves our attention are the more than ten paintings drawn by Japanese elementary school students. Japanese education emphasizes the training of national patriotism, from kindergarten to university, all with this as the main purpose. Therefore, after the Japanese army invaded our territory, the elementary school teachers in their country ordered children to draw cartoons that could stimulate the patriotism of the soldiers, and sent them to the army as a form of consolation. The items displayed at Jinan University were drawn by students from a certain Japanese elementary school and sent to the 19th Regiment. Some depict the Japanese flag flying in the wind, some depict Japanese soldiers holding guns, and some depict the killing of Chinese soldiers. In short, the intention is to stimulate the patriotism of the soldiers.

Morbid State

— Chuan Yun

丨Prescribing the Right Medicine丨

Wearing a new camel-hair robe, feeling warm all over, yet meeting people and shouting desperately: "How cold it is! The poor Northeastern Volunteer Army, in the snow, holding stiff guns, fighting, fighting..." Yet one's own hands are in one's pockets, with such a leisurely attitude. Talking is probably the only forte of the Chinese!

×　×　×　×

Sitting on the tram, one shouts: "When women come, you must give up your seat!" But before one's eyes, on one's knees, are trembling, crowded, thin, annoying, old women or men. Yet one sits there calmly, thinking: "How annoying, always crowding in here!"

×　×　×　×

How enthusiastic! On the streets, in the newspapers, one can see stores holding big sales, and the sales are also donating to the Volunteer Army. Thus, posters saying "Buy one more item, save one more life" are pasted in colorful splendor on the glass counters. Buying one more item can certainly save one more life, but how many percent is added to an item, and is it necessarily going to have such a great effect?

×　×　×　×

The newspapers publish donation announcements, stirring up only a few initiators. The advertisements of the three major film companies in the cinemas, however, stir up tens of thousands of compatriots, buying, buying desperately, not caring about the money! The same newspaper, carrying large advertisements, yet, yet the result is like this!

×　×　×　×

Women themselves are shouting for liberation, and others are also advocating for them. On the surface, if we casually walk into an organization, we can always see a few female staff members. Indeed, this is an achievement of liberation. However, the gossip about the "flower vase" in the organization is still prevalent. The female comrades, however, are so complacent, admitting, "If it weren't for liberation, how could I have a job? And such a leisurely job?"

The Industry of Intellectuals

— Tao Zai Dong

Since Tianxu used his skills to create Invincible Brand Tooth Powder, adding glory to national products and redeeming his status as a scholar through industry, public opinion has praised him. At the same time, there was Ding Rong. Ding Xu, as advertised in various newspapers, is the Hunan specialty exclusively sold by Changsha Huaxin Down Company 丨 Duck bedding and pillows. The function of down is not only to keep warm, but also to be a tool for floating on water. Its widespread sales throughout the country and gradual export have become an industry. More than ten years ago, this product simply did not exist. The creator, Deng Ming, was Ding Peng, courtesy name Tuanjiu, from Hengshan County, Hunan. His grandfather and great-grandfather were both members of the Hanlin Academy. After becoming officials, they returned to their hometowns and ran academies, passing down Confucianism through their family. Tuanjiu was a student in the county and graduated from Normal University, serving in the education field with distinction. In his spare time, he studied the manufacture of duck down, repeatedly failing and losing money, with relatives and friends laughing at him. Tuanjiu persevered and finally succeeded, obtaining a special permit from the government. From then on, the term "Ding Rong" spread. In saying this, it is believed that studying should seek useful knowledge. It is hoped that the intelligence and talent of our youth should be used in useful industrial and commercial enterprises. Being just a writer is not enough. One must be like Chen Xuyuan and Ding Tuanjiu to be worthy of being called an intellectual.

The True Reclusive Flower

— Shi Yu

丨Still in the Human World丨

Mr. Cheng Zhanlu calls the current chrysanthemums "political figures among flowers." Even if the colorful hundreds of varieties of famous chrysanthemums were to turn into people, grow mouths, they could not strongly argue with old Cheng. However, there is a type of chrysanthemum that does not deserve blame. It still possesses the high spirit and refined taste of reclusion, preserving the proper color of "gathering yellow flowers" from that year. Even if the old master of the eastern fence were reborn today, he would not feel any shame in front of it. Moreover, Zhou Maoshu, upon seeing it, would still call it the "reclusive flower." Because it originally does not want to be among the grand chrysanthemum gatherings. And the chrysanthemum gatherings do not need it either. Those tea houses, restaurants, and theaters; it certainly would never set foot in them its entire life, let alone anything else. Where exactly is this type of chrysanthemum? It's just that Brother Zhanlu is always in his study in the city, and hasn't gone to wander in the desolate countryside, so he naturally wouldn't encounter the truly old-fashioned reclusive flower. However, this truly old-fashioned reclusive flower has long been criticized by people by adding a word to it, calling it "wild chrysanthemum." It's as if people who are used to showing off now see a simply dressed, honest, and experienced person, and refuse to give him a civilized title, but want to privately bestow the uncivilized word "wild" upon him. Little do they know that the wild chrysanthemum, which the world doesn't value, its flowers and leaves can be used to make medicine and treat illnesses. It's not like the colorful, political-natured chrysanthemums, which, besides being used for people to play with, have no other use. Therefore, I want to specially bring it up and tell people about it. Since Brother Zhanlu used the words "political figures among flowers" to ridicule chrysanthemums, he must have nothing but love and respect for the truly old-fashioned reclusive flower. Brother Zhanlu must also say that I almost forgot; I almost forgot; isn't that so?

Brief News

— Ming Xin

The colleagues of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railways, in order to support the Northeastern Volunteer Army, will hold theatrical performances at the Sanxing Stage on the 14th and 15th of this month to raise funds. The tickets are divided into three types: two yuan, one yuan, and five jiao. A total of more than 5,000 tickets have been issued, and the audience has been completely full for two days. The plays performed were all of high quality, especially the fact that some well-known women, who usually do not perform easily, were able to generously sacrifice their beauty, which was most commendable. It is also learned that the colleagues of the railway will continue to perform in the capital for two days, still appealing for the Northeastern Volunteer Army.

The Crossroads of Death (16)

— Fan Yanqiao

She didn't want to; she was afraid that using her real surname would lead people to investigate and find out about her background. It was a pity that her parents had passed away early, and she had no close relatives. Only then did she become someone's adopted daughter-in-law. She was very young at the time, so she didn't remember her surname. This was a matter of careful consideration. After much deliberation, she chose the most luxurious surname in modern times from the Hundred Family Surnames, and took the surname Jiang.

Again, the gossip magazine contributors were busy, taking photos, printing business cards, writing promotional materials, recognizing a "sugar daddy," one by one, step by step. Soon, she became popular, almost overshadowing the old pro 丨 Little Pearl 丨. Sure enough, as Little Pearl had expected, she didn't have to worry about food, clothing, or housing. Those willing to provide for her were endless, and she was worried that she couldn't accept all their kindness. Indeed, the clothes in the four small suitcases she brought were no longer needed. Whether it was raining or late, without makeup, she would occasionally throw something on, but she was still afraid of being caught by uninvited guests, causing them to gossip. She really sent them all to the pawnshop. Little Pearl said to her:

"Are you really willing to throw away a pair of silk stockings? I'm afraid they were bought just the day before yesterday."

Ai Li said, "There's a small hole in them, can't wear them anymore."

Little Pearl said, "When I was in Suzhou, I still saw you using a hook to pull threads from a torn sock to patch a hole in a new sock. Could it be that you've forgotten already, after being in Shanghai for less than three months?"

Ai Meng gave Little Pearl a cigarette, lit one for herself, sat on the sofa, tilted her head back, pursed her lips, and exhaled circles of smoke, smiling with her cheeks puffed out. After a long time, she said:

"People are cheap. I think those who wear 26-yuan-a-pair silk stockings are even more wasteful than us."

Ai Gu had fallen deeply in love with Ai Li. Everything had changed except for a scar about half an inch from her left eyebrow, which, although covered by her hair, would inadvertently show. This was indelible. It was the scar she got when she was ten years old, chasing water in Cuiwei Village, and was stabbed by A Gen's bamboo pole.

Commercial News

Financial Swap Gold Market Stabilized

Education News

Important News Bandit Suppression Headquarters Resolves Educational Unrest in Hubei Province

Order to Resume Classes Within One Week; Funds Will Not Be Issued to Those Who Do Not Resume

Hankou, 16th - The Bandit Suppression Headquarters issued an order on the 15th to the joint conference of various schools and museums and the joint association of teachers and staff to clear the arrears according to the original method. After the provincial government implements the new budget this month, the educational funds will be issued in two installments per month. It is hoped that the importance of education and the vitality of the local area will be taken into account, and classes will be fully resumed within this week. If classes are not resumed for one day, funds will not be issued for one day.

Director of Gansu Education Department Resigns

Unable to Cope with Petition for Strike by Various Schools

Lanzhou, 16th - After the teachers of various secondary schools went on strike, they decided to petition the Provincial Education Department. The Director of the Education Department, Shui Zi, was unable to cope and expressed his resignation.

Peking University's New Construction Plan Finalized

Jiang Menglin Returns to Peiping to Report

Beiping, 16th - Jiang Menglin returned to Peiping at noon today. Regarding the repayment of arrears and the new construction plan for Peking University, a result has been negotiated with the Ministry of Education. A Peking University school affairs meeting will be convened within days to report on the process of contacting Beijing.

Ministry of Education to Organize

Compilation Committee for Curriculum Standards for Civilian Schools

Regarding the curriculum standards for ordinary education in primary and secondary schools and kindergartens, the Ministry of Education has been employing experts to study and review them for years, and the curriculum standards have been promulgated. The curriculum standards for mass school nuclei in social education have not yet been established. Moreover, the promotion of social education in various provinces and cities has made progress in recent years. In addition to ordinary primary mass schools, more than ten provinces and cities have established advanced mass schools. In order to unify the curriculum standards so that there is a basis for reference and connection, the compilation of curriculum standards is urgent. It is reported that the Ministry of Education is now planning to organize a compilation committee for the curriculum standards of mass schools in order to employ experts who have studied mass education for a long time to engage in the establishment of appropriate mass curriculum standards.

The C Type of the Three People's Principles Thousand-Character Textbook Has Been Printed

The temporary edition of the Three People's Principles Thousand-Character Textbook, types A, B, and C (type A focuses on adults, type B is for children) has been promulgated and implemented. The existing type C (focusing on rural areas) has been signed and noted by the Central Propaganda Department and sent to the Ministry of Education. It is reported that the Ministry of Education will order the provinces and cities to implement it after the printing is completed.

Local

Chinese Educational Society National School Supplies Exhibition

To Be Held from December 25th to 27th

The Chinese Educational Society will hold a National School Supplies Exhibition in December, bringing together national education experts to observe and promote national school supplies. The methods are recorded as follows: Article 1: The purpose of this society is to observe and promote national school supplies. Article 2: The exhibits of this society are limited to the following five types of purely national products: 1. Animal, plant, and mineral specimens 2. Teaching aids for mathematics, physics, and chemistry 3. Teaching aids for science, agriculture, engineering, medicine, etc. 4. Woolen cloth that can be used for student uniforms 5. Children's toys. If this society considers that there is no need to display the items in the preceding paragraph, it may notify the company in advance or temporarily to remove them. Article 3: All shops and factories participating in the exhibition must register with the society in writing before December 15th of this year, and indicate the following points: 1. Type of product, 2. Number of products, 3. Shop and factory name, 4. Shop and factory location, 5. Person in charge of visiting the exhibition. Article 4: All exhibits must be affixed with labels, and the shops and factories must fill in the following points separately: 1. Name, 2. Price 3. Place of origin, 4. Remarks Article 5: The exhibition methods are as follows: 1. The transportation and display of objects are the responsibility of the shops and factories themselves. 2. The exhibition area is determined by drawing lots. 3. Exhibits must be displayed and withdrawn within the dates specified by the society. Article 6: The exhibition date is set from 8:00 am on December 25th to 5:00 pm on the 27th. Article 7: The society will not comment on or retain the exhibits.

Council Meeting of the Municipal Education Association

▲Discuss Matters Entrusted by the Delegates' Congress

▲Issue a Declaration to Aid Private Schools in the French Concession

The Municipal Education Association held its third council meeting at its association premises on Wenmiao Road at 4:00 pm yesterday. Those present were Zhou Feicheng, Zhang Zaibo, Huang Zao Xiong, Ma Jiazhen, Xu Zeyi, Wu Xiu, Zhang Zhongdao, Tao Baichuan, Chen Jicheng, etc. Those attending were Zhou Darong, Wu Renqi, Zhang Yousan, Mao Yun, etc. Chairman Zhou Feicheng, Recorder Liu Shunzai, opened the meeting as usual to discuss matters: 1. What should be done about the stagnation of the work of the education associations in the fourth and sixth districts? It was resolved that they should be reorganized and reported separately to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Education Bureau for approval. 2. Cases handed over to the council by the Delegates' Congress: 1. Broadly raise funds for education in this city, establish schools, and increase the regular expenses of public and private schools to seek student fees. It was resolved to submit the case to the Education Bureau for approval. 2. Submit a request to the Party and government agencies to plan to revitalize education in the war zone. It was resolved to submit the case to the Party and government agencies for approval. 3. Draft a ten-year education plan for Greater Shanghai and submit it to the Party and government agencies for adoption and implementation. It was resolved to appoint Tao Baichuan, Zhang Zhongdao, Zheng Hongnian, Cheng Kuanzhi, and four directors to draft it.

Joint Association of Private Schools in the French Concession

Declaration Demanding Subsidies to Develop Education

▲20% of the French Concession's Income Should Be Used for Chinese Education Expenses

The Joint Association of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession of this city issued a declaration to request the French Public Works Bureau to develop Chinese education in the concession, stating:

"Since the opening of Shanghai as a port and the establishment of concessions by the French, more than 80 years have passed. The entire facilities of the concession need not be discussed too much. Just in terms of the tax obligations fulfilled by our Chinese people, the accumulated years have been enormous. According to reason and sentiment, our Chinese people should have the right to enjoy equality. However, the fact is greatly different. For education, which is considered the most important relationship for our people, very little attention is paid. Our national government, with the tax revenue of the concession in the hands of the French, is also limited by its economic power and cannot pay much attention. A small number of private schools have been established, but they are all unable to expand due to financial exhaustion, causing numerous students to have no way to study. This is indeed what our people are deeply dissatisfied with and cannot help but say. According to the latest statistics from the French Public Works Bureau, the population of the French Concession totals 479,571 people, of which Chinese account for 462,342 people, and the number of school-age children is as high as 128,437. Western children account for only 2,737 people. According to the 1932 budget of the French Public Works Bureau, the total annual income is approximately 6,921,732 taels. With such a large number of school-age children, how much funding should be used to establish how many schools, and how many Chinese children's schools should be re-established so that Chinese children will no longer sigh that they have no education? However, the French Public Works Bureau has failed to take this into account. In a jurisdiction with so many school-age children and such a large total annual tax revenue, it has only allocated 218,200 taels for education expenses and established three or four schools. It is estimated that Western public schools account for 130,000 taels, the Sino-French Academy accounts for 60,000 taels, and the newly established Chinese children's primary schools account for approximately 20,000 taels. Schools that are exempt from donations account for 8,200 taels. From this point of view, 24. Supervise and urge the government to recover the educational rights of the concession. It was resolved to submit the case to the Education Bureau. 5. Request the Public Works Bureau to exempt the advertising tax and handling fees for schools established with the approval of the Education Bureau. It was resolved to send a letter to the Public Works Bureau for approval. 3. Draft work plans for each department. It was resolved that the heads of each department should draft them within one week. 4. Appoint persons in charge of each group of the Research Committee. It was resolved to appoint Zheng Hongnian for the university education group, Tao Baichuan for the secondary school education group, Wu Xiu for the primary school education group, and Zhang Zaibo for the social education group. 5. The Joint Association of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession sent a letter requesting that the French Concession Public Works Bureau unanimously allocate 20% of all income to Chinese education expenses. It was resolved that: 1. A letter should be sent to the Chinese directors of the French Municipal Council to strive for it. 2. A declaration should be issued. The meeting was adjourned after the discussion."

Legal and Health Counselor Meeting Held by the Vocational Guidance Institute

Last night at 6 p.m., the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute of the China Vocational Education Society invited health counselors Song Guobin, Wang Yugang, Zeng Lixun, Ge Chenghui, Zhang Zhongming, Chen Bangdian, Huang Yixiang, Yang Baohang, Wang Zhenchuan, Xu Jihua, legal counselors Zhu Shaowen, Shan Yuhua, Qian Jianqiu, Wang Zhengshao, Yu Zhijiang, Yuan Yang'an, Li Zhongdao, Peng Yanghou, Huang Zixiong, etc., to hold a joint meeting at Jue Lin Vegetarian Restaurant. The director of the society, Mr. Jiang Wenyu, presided over the meeting and delivered a speech, welcoming the counselors present and thanking them for their enthusiasm in guiding young people. Then, the deputy director, Mr. Yang Weiyu, delivered a speech with the same meaning. Next, the director of the institute, Hua Zhanen Pan Yangyao, reported on the progress of health and legal guidance at the institute in the past three years. In general, legal matters mainly involved divorce and inheritance cases, while health matters mainly involved sexual neurasthenia. Then, Wang Yugang, Zhu Shaowen, Li Zhongdao, and Shan Yuhua successively expressed their opinions, mainly as follows: (1) Dr. Wang Yugang advocated that young people who seek health guidance before becoming ill should be considered within the scope of health guidance, and the health counselors invited by the institute should provide guidance once a month. The names of all counselors and the dates and times should be disclosed by the institute in advance. Young people who are already ill and seek guidance should be considered as seeking disease guidance, which is not within the scope of health guidance, and should be referred by the institute to the counselors' clinics for diagnosis and treatment, with preferential treatment. (2) Lawyer Li Zhongdao advocated that legal issues should be divided into two categories: legal guidance and legal aid. Before the court trial, mediation work should be tried first. Shan Yuhua also supported this proposal. Finally, Zhu Shaowen was publicly recommended to draft a declaration on legal issues, hoping that young people would take divorce issues seriously. Mr. Jiang Wenyu, based on the diagnoses of various doctors, noted that in recent years, young students have been fond of reading erotic books and improper publications and enjoy talking about love, leading to an increasing number of cases of sexual neurasthenia. He drafted a declaration advising young people to pay attention to their health, hoping that young people would be alert. All the above issues were unanimously approved, and the meeting ended happily at 9 p.m.

Wu Jingxiong Lectures on the Art of Life

At the Civic Education Center on the 20th of This Month

Of the 777 Western children, the educational expenses account for 130,000 taels, while the educational expenses for the 125,700 Chinese children of school age account for only 88,200 taels. What injustice in the world is greater than this? Moreover, Chinese people pay more than two-thirds of the entire French Concession's tax revenue. Now that the French Municipal Council is so indifferent to Chinese education, we cannot help but feel regret and deep dissatisfaction. According to the annual report of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, the total annual regular income is 15,537,220 taels, of which 1,186,920 taels are for Chinese education. Calculated proportionally, the French Municipal Council should allocate 5,287,666 taels for Chinese education. If we further calculate based on the 160,000 school-age children in the International Settlement and the current proportion of Chinese educational expenses, the French Municipal Council should allocate 9,089,050 taels for Chinese education. In comparison, the French Municipal Council's improper allocation is already obvious. Furthermore, we cannot be satisfied with the public concession's current facilities for Chinese education. In summary, we believe that developing Chinese education in the French Concession is an urgent task and a right that Chinese people in the French Concession should enjoy, and it is also a responsibility that the French Municipal Council should bear. For the current plan, the French Municipal Council should, at a minimum, allocate 20% of its total annual income to Chinese educational expenses. On the one hand, supplement the established private schools to seek expansion, and on the other hand, gradually increase the number of Chinese children's schools to seek universal education. The members of this association, bearing the important responsibility of education and witnessing this situation, cannot sit idly by. Therefore, we hereby initiate a request, hoping that people from all walks of life will provide assistance, and we especially hope that the Chinese directors and Chinese committee members will make a loud call to promote its realization. The members of this association especially vow to work tirelessly to promote the education of Chinese children. This is our declaration.

The third academic lecture at the Civic Education Center was previously scheduled to be given by Dr. Wu Jingxiong on the Art of Life. However, due to Wu's illness, the lecture could not be held. It has now been rescheduled to be given in the lecture hall of the center at 10 a.m. on the 20th of this month (Sunday). All previously issued tickets will remain valid. Those who have not yet received tickets can pick them up at the center's office starting today.

Regulations of the National Games Preparatory Committee Announced Yesterday

The Committee Consists of Fifteen to Twenty-One Members

Nanjing, 16th (Electrical Transmission) The Ministry of Education announced the organizational regulations of the Preparatory Committee for the 22nd National Games, totaling 13 articles. The regulations stipulate the responsibilities, which are to receive and manage the Central Sports Field, prepare for the opening ceremony, handle the affairs during the opening ceremony, and report on the conclusion after the opening ceremony. The committee will have 15 to 21 members, 3 standing committee members, and 1 chief executive officer. There will also be 5 groups: general affairs, engineering, regulations, competition, and reception. Each group will have 1 director and several staff members.

Local News

This City's Reconstruction Public Bonds Underwritten by British Merchants

Director Cai Issues Statement

Reports state that the Shanghai Reconstruction Public Bonds Regulations have been amended and passed by the Legislative Yuan, and the underwriting contract has also been signed. Yesterday, reporters from various newspapers inquired with the Finance Bureau about the underwriting situation. Director Cai issued the following statement:

(1) The public bonds, totaling 6 million yuan, are underwritten by the British firm Lih An & Co. of Shanghai, and the HSBC Bank is entrusted to manage the repayment of principal and interest. The municipal government will receive 80% of the face value in real terms, amounting to 4.8 million silver dollars. (2) After Lih An & Co. pays the amount of the underwriting, the municipal government will not interfere with how they promote the bonds. It is estimated that the firm will sell them at 85% of the face value, as the firm must bear all promotional expenses, such as advertising (the city's previous issuance of public bonds also incurred tens of thousands of dollars in expenses) and broker commissions. Therefore, the bond price must be increased slightly. (According to market practice, broker commissions are usually around 2% to 4%. The Shanghai Telephone Company's issuance of 20 million taels of public bonds had broker commissions ranging from 2% to 4%.) In the future, as the city's external credit improves, the selling price of these public bonds may continue to rise, exceeding 85%, which is also expected. (3) In the past decade or so, the HSBC Bank has rarely managed Chinese bonds. This time, the city's bonds are underwritten by Lih An & Co., and the HSBC Bank is managing the repayment of principal and interest, which shows that the bank is well aware of the common economic interests and is able to cooperate. In the future, the city's construction projects will flourish, and we will rely heavily on the support of Chinese and foreign banking groups. This is just one aspect. (4) It is rare for Chinese domestic bonds to be underwritten by foreign merchants. Shanghai's initiative will excite foreigners' investment ideas, and various domestic bonds will be positively affected. (5) The public bonds have a term of 20 years for complete repayment.

The interest rate is 7%. Lih An & Co. underwrites at 80% of the face value and pays the full amount without any commission. From the date of underwriting to the date of full repayment, the average annual interest rate is approximately 0.070668. In other words, the municipal government's average annual interest rate for using the bond proceeds is also 0.070668. However, if Lih An & Co. sells the bonds at 85% of the face value, the average annual interest rate for investors would be 0.09589. Although some domestic bonds have been issued at full price or at 98% of the face value, the highest opening price on the market is only around 70% to 80%. Recently, it has fallen to only 40% to 50%. According to the market price, the interest rate is already more than 1% per month. Therefore, the interest rate for this issuance of public bonds cannot be too low. However, calculated at the above average annual interest rate, it is already much lower than various other bonds. (6) The city is issuing public bonds this time because citizens lack the ability to subscribe after the devastation of the war. Therefore, we are not soliciting subscriptions from citizens. This point was discussed in detail in the previous statement. As for the domestic banking sector, it was also reported by the Central News Agency that due to the severe financial constraints after the war, there was no surplus capacity to underwrite these public bonds. Therefore, we negotiated with foreign merchants to underwrite the bonds, which is essentially indirectly utilizing foreign capital. Although the use of foreign capital to handle municipal affairs is not common in China, there are many precedents in other countries. Before World War I, Japan issued bonds to Europe and the United States to alleviate financial difficulties and reconstruct Tokyo after the earthquake. Furthermore, many state-owned enterprises used foreign capital. Before World War I, the United States built railways with funds from Britain. Japan invested in South Manchuria and obtained special rights, mostly funded by Britain and the United States. Currently, Taiwan borrowed tens of millions of dollars from the New York copper syndicate Morgan & Co. to develop its electricity industry. These are just a few examples.

Board of Directors of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Decides to

Form a Debt Restructuring Committee

Promote Qian Xinzhi and Li Fuxun to Draft the Charter

American Merchants Send Another Letter Continuing Their Protest

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Board of Directors of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company held its second meeting to discuss the restructuring steps. It was decided to form a "Debt Restructuring Committee" and promote Directors Qian Xinzhi and Li Fuxun to draft the organizational charter. The details are recorded as follows:

Board of Directors Meeting Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the second Board of Directors meeting was held. Shi Liangcai, Zhang Shouyong, Ye Zhuotang, Yang Zhixiong, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Guangfu, Hu Bijang, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Sheng Lanchen, General Manager Liu Hongsheng, Zhang Gongquan, and others attended. Wang Xiaolai and Yu Rizhang were absent due to other commitments. Director Zhang Shouyong was elected chairman. First, General Manager Liu reported on the negotiations to recover the four wharves and dispatched personnel to maintain the current situation. Next, the board discussed the company's restructuring steps. All directors agreed that this matter was of great importance and decided to form a "China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Debt Restructuring Committee." Directors Qian Xinzhi and Li Fuxun were elected to draft the organizational charter in advance, which will be approved at the third Board of Directors meeting to ensure its early establishment. Afterwards, other important matters were discussed, and the meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM.

Shi Liangcai's Statement Standing Director Shi Liangcai told a Central News Agency reporter that the acquisition of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's shares and the mortgage of the three wharves are matters related to the government after the company was brought under state ownership. The Ministry of Communications will be in charge, so the Board of Directors has not discussed it. As for the company's recovery of the three wharves from the American-owned China 영업 Co., the company has raised protests, and the Western press in Shanghai has criticized the company for not understanding the truth and for monitoring Li Guojie without submitting him to the court for investigation, which seems to be contrary to the rule of law. In fact, Li Guojie's temporary monitoring will only last until the government decides on a solution, whether to hand him over to the court for trial or to be handled by the government. The takeover of the three wharves was to prevent accidents involving all the workers. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company had previously borrowed 5 million taels from HSBC Bank and owed more than 2 million taels in salt tax interest and subsidies, totaling more than 7 million taels, which urgently needed to be repaid. Therefore, HSBC Bank, as the first creditor, had a claim on the wharves. If the 10 million taels mortgage from the China 영업 Co. were added, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company would have been completely bankrupt. The vast majority of coolies and laborers who depend on it for a living would have lost their jobs, and China's shipping industry would have been completely ruined. Therefore, this decisive action was taken out of necessity.

Liu Hongsheng's Statement General Manager Liu Hongsheng told a New Voice News reporter that yesterday's report stating that his office was illegally seized was a misunderstanding. He only acknowledges this mortgage procedure if it is legal. Legality, in commercial terms, means that it should be approved by the shareholders' meeting. In political terms, such a major event should be approved by the Executive Yuan. Whether the mortgage of the four wharves has gone through this procedure is worth investigating.

Takeover Not Yet Completed Although the Board of Directors has taken over the company, the various documents have not yet been finalized. A detailed inventory will be taken after meeting with Li Guojie. The Industrial Property Section has not been fully taken over due to its close relationship with the Jiyu Real Estate Company. As for the Supervisory Committee, it has started working at the old site of the Supervisory Office, and the Board of Directors has started working at the old site of the former Board of Directors.

American Merchants Protest Yesterday, the company continued to receive protest letters from the American-owned China 영업 Co., continuing to state that they are not giving up their rights under the contract and urging the company to send someone to take responsibility and negotiate various procedures or settle the case. It is reported that the Board of Directors discussed this case yesterday and decided to submit it to the Ministry for instructions on how to handle it.

The Ruikang Steamer Makes Every Effort to Rescue

According to a telegram from the Shanghai Coastal Radio Station at 11:20 PM last night, the Fuqing steamer caught fire outside the Wusong Estuary, and the situation was urgent. News at 1:00 AM this morning All passengers and crew have been rescued and sent to Shanghai by the Ruikang steamer. However, the entire Fuqing steamer has been destroyed.

More Than Five Hundred Villagers from Pengpu District

Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday

Yu Hongjun Expresses that a Telegram has been Sent to the Ministry of Railways

Hoping to Achieve the Goal of Avoiding the Village

More than 500 villagers from Pengpu District, because their residences have been designated by the Ministry of Railways as the site for the construction of a new station, and survey stakes have been hammered in, causing fear and anxiety, specially went to the Municipal Government to petition yesterday.

Petition Situation More than 500 villagers from Pengpu District, yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, supported the elderly and carried the young, and submitted a petition, went to the Municipal Government to petition. They elected Hou Xuanqing, Zhao Youting, Zhao Youxiu, Zhang Zhongxiang and other four representatives to enter, the rest were waiting in the open space in front of the Municipal Government.
