The Post-War Relief Committee Begins Lending Capital to the Poor

It Will Take About Four Days to Complete

Total Amount is 15,000 Yuan

The Shanghai Municipal Post-War Relief Committee, in order to restore the prosperity of the war-torn areas and to help the affected poor households to rebuild their businesses, has established a temporary lending office in Minli Road, Zhabei, and has established branches in six rural areas, including Jiangwan, Wusong, Zhenru, Pengpu, Yinxing, and Yinxiang, to handle various lending and borrowing matters. Since registration began, more than 300 poor households have borrowed capital. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the first batch of capital was lent to the poor.

Lending Measures The temporary relief lending measures are divided into (A) housing loans, (B) capital for the poor, (C) capital for small industries, and (D) repair loans for charitable organizations. As for the repayment period, the capital for the poor has a term of one year, housing loans and capital for small industries have a term of four years, and repair loans for charitable organizations have a term of six years. Poor people whose houses were destroyed by artillery fire during the war and are unable to rebuild, small industries that suffered losses in the war and cannot be maintained, and poor people in the disaster area can apply for loans after completing the loan procedures at the office. After the office investigates and confirms, the loans will be issued. The prescribed amounts are as follows: (1) Housing loans are limited to 50 yuan to 200 yuan per person. (2) Capital for the poor is limited to 10 yuan to 20 yuan per person. (3) Capital for small industries is limited to 50 yuan to 500 yuan per person. (4) Repair loans for charitable organizations will be determined separately.

Lending Situation Yesterday, more than 100 poor people received capital from the office. The loan procedures for these poor people have been completed, and each person received 20 silver dollars. The capital lending to the poor will take about four days to complete, with a total amount of 15,000 yuan, of which 4,300 yuan will be distributed to Zhabei District, and the remainder will be distributed to the six districts of Zhenru, etc. The capital lending to small industries will also be issued in about ten days, with a total amount of 40,000 yuan, of which 19,000 yuan will be distributed to Zhabei District, and the remainder will also be distributed to various districts. Housing loans are mostly in Wusong and Jiangwan. Each borrower has completed all the procedures with Mr. Wang Binze, and the total number will be reported and the loans will be issued on a fixed date, which will be in two weeks.

Disaster Relief Committee Surveys the Yangtze River's New Embankment

▲Invites Chinese and Foreign Celebrities▲ The Emei Steamer ▲Scheduled to Depart from Shanghai▲

Last year's flood disaster caused most of the Yangtze River embankments to be destroyed. The National Government's Flood Relief Committee was established and decided to use the "work-for-relief" method, using American wheat to build river embankments. The lower reaches start from Shierxu and the upper reaches end at Shashi, extending for more than 6,000 miles, employing 600,000 disaster workers and setting up ten offices. The construction of new embankments began in October last year and has now been completed. The unfinished projects of the Flood Relief Committee are now being taken over by the National Economic Council. Fourteen work-for-relief bureaus have been closed one after another, and four bureaus, including the Jianghan Bureau and the Jiangxi Bureau, are still remaining. The remaining funds from the relief wheat are now being used for dredging the Huai River's outer river and repairing embankments. The Flood Relief Committee believes that the new river embankment has been completed, so that even if the river water rises

Page 14

to forty feet, it will still not overflow and destroy the embankment. Tens of thousands of acres of farmland near the embankment in Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces will become fertile land in the future. The annual grain and agricultural products can be increased by tens of millions of yuan compared to the previous year, which can directly increase the wealth of the people and indirectly reduce bandits. The committee specially invited important figures from all walks of life in Shanghai to inspect the Yangtze River and inspect the current situation of the Yangtze River in order to plan further construction. The committee invited ten Westerners and forty celebrities from all walks of life in China, as well as the heads of the construction departments of Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces, and Xin Bosheng and others, to go together. Yesterday, the committee specially chartered the Emei steamer from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to carry Chinese and foreign guests to inspect the Yangtze River embankment project. The round trip is scheduled for three weeks. The Emei steamer is specially undergoing repairs at the factory and is scheduled to depart on the 26th, starting from the Shierxu section and ending at Shashi. After the inspection is completed, the steamer will return to Shanghai. The invitation cards have been issued.

Bandit Suppression Headquarters

Reviews the Additional Disaster Relief Donations on Road and Telegraph Fees

Chiang Kai-shek Replies to the Three Provinces' Relief Association by Telegram

Has Telegraphed to the Executive Yuan to Instruct Relevant Departments to Comply

The Shanghai Provisional Relief Association for Disaster Areas in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei telegraphed General Commander Chiang on the 25th of last month, requesting him to find a way to add disaster relief donations to the road and telegraph fees. Yesterday, it received Chiang's reply by telegram. There have been many requests for disaster relief from various places. The following is a summary:

Additional Disaster Relief Donations on Road and Telegraph Fees The association received a reply by telegram from General Commander Chiang of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, saying: "I have received and respectfully read the telegraph. The recovered bandit areas in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are in urgent need of relief. The government's proposal to add disaster relief donations to the road and telegraph fees is an essential measure. This headquarters has reviewed the various sections opened in the original telegraph and telegraphed to the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications to comply. I am attaching a copy of the original telegram for your information. Chiang Kai-shek [seal]" A copy of the original telegram from this headquarters to the Executive Yuan is attached. "To President Song of the Executive Yuan: According to a telegraph from Xu Minying, Vice Chairman Wang Zhen, Wang Xiaolai, and others of the Shanghai Provisional Relief Association for Disaster Areas in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei, the recovered bandit areas in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are in urgent need of relief. They proposed to add disaster relief donations to the road and telegraph fees. After reviewing the various proposed methods separately, this department has determined the following: (1) The original telegram requested that disaster relief donations be added to long-distance passenger tickets on national railways, with 40 cents for first class, 20 cents for second class, and 10 cents for first class. It is proposed to follow the plan for first class, change the first class to 30 cents, and change the third class to 5 cents. The economic strength of third-class passengers is weaker, and ticket prices have been increased repeatedly in recent years. Calculated as a percentage, the increase is already higher than that of first and second classes, so it is not appropriate to add more. (2) The original telegram requested that disaster relief donations be added to freight transport on the Pinghan Railway, with 5% for salt and coal and 2.1% for other goods. It is found that freight transport on the Pinghan Railway is now dispersed by the Longhai Line and Huaiyun, and the commerce of Hankou is depressed. This is also one of the reasons, so it is not appropriate to increase freight rates again and hinder freight transport. Moreover, to develop the rural economy of Henan and Hubei, it is necessary to reduce freight rates and facilitate trade. This item should not be discussed. (3) The original telegram requested that disaster relief donations be added to telegrams, regardless of wired or wireless or distance, with 5 cents added to each telegram. It is found that adding donations to telegrams has little relationship with the livelihood of the people, so it seems possible to follow the plan. (4) The original telegram requested that the effective period for adding disaster relief donations be limited to six months. It is found that the planned period of six months is not too long, so it seems possible to follow the plan. However, it should be stated that it should be revoked immediately after the deadline. The above-discussed methods are enclosed with the original telegram and submitted to your esteemed yuan for review and to instruct the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications to comply. Chiang Kai-shek [seal]"

Anhui Organizes Relief Group The association received an official letter from Wu Zhongxin, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, saying: "We have approved your letter instructing us to appoint local impartial gentry, merchants, and enthusiastic people to organize a relief group. We have submitted it to the committee's talks, and it was decided that the fundraising group should be established as soon as possible. The people's department will draw up the charter and submit it for approval. We have instructed the relevant departments to comply and request your review. "

Henan Relief Council Asks for Relief Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Relief Council, telegraphed: "It has been approved that the Henan Provincial Government's letter opens, it has been approved that General Commander Chiang's secret telegram opens, and it has been learned that Xu, Commissioner of the Ninth District of Henan, telegraphed that the refugees in Xinji have no food and no shelter and are in urgent need of relief. In addition to submitting the report, we respectfully submit this telegram and request a large sum of relief money quickly." In addition, the Henan Provincial Government replied, stating that they have approved the instructions to appoint local impartial silk merchants to jointly initiate the organization of a fundraising group and have instructed the provincial relief council to handle it as soon as possible.

The Party Department of the Division Asks for Relief A telegram from the Special Party Department of the 32nd Division of the Army stated: "We respectfully represent the 200,000 disaster victims in Zhongshan and sincerely appeal to you to open your purses and save them in order to save the remnants of the disaster."

Meeting to be Called Tomorrow The association sent letters to the inspection teams and preparatory committee members, saying: "We respectfully inform you that on the 15th of this month, representatives of various groups at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce discussed the organizational charter of the inspection team for the disaster areas in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei and decided to pass it with revisions. The following three proposals were also decided: (1) The minimum amount of the first disaster relief fund for the three provinces is tentatively set at 150,000 yuan. (2) The government is requested to allocate relief funds first for disaster relief by this association (3) The preparatory committee is notified to inform the legal groups to recommend one to three representatives as members of the inspection team within one week, etc. We have set the second preparatory committee meeting for 4:00 PM on the 18th of this month (Friday) at the Renji Pawnshop, where this association is located. There are important motions that need to be discussed and decided. We have enclosed the revised organizational charter and sent this letter for your attention. We respectfully request that you attend the meeting at the time."

Typhoon Destroys Dongsha Island Lighthouse

Attention Mariners

Typhoons have struck Luzon, Taiwan, and eastern Japan, causing extensive damage. The South China Sea has also been affected. It is reported that Dongsha Island, located near 116 degrees 43 minutes East longitude and 23 degrees 21 minutes North latitude, was hit by a severe typhoon and massive waves. A lighthouse built by the Coast Guard was struck by the high winds and waves and has been destroyed. The light on the tower is no longer functioning as a navigational aid. Upon learning of the incident, the Coast Guard immediately received a wireless report and has dispatched a large number of workers for repairs. Meanwhile, the Hydrographic Office has issued Temporary Notice No. 112, informing all shipping companies to take note. Vessels navigating in the area should consult British Admiralty charts No. 361, 2661B, and 1263.

Mr. Song Ziwen, Acting President of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 1:30 PM via a Sikorsky aircraft from Nanjing, accompanied by his secretary, Huang Chun-dao. He immediately returned to his residence to rest.

British House of Commons

Discussion on Shanghai Special District Court Issue

A Reuters dispatch from London on the 15th reports that the issue of the Shanghai Special District Court was recently raised in the House of Commons and was discussed again today in the House of Lords. Earl Peel read a motion, requesting attention to the agreement establishing the court and inquiring what steps the government is currently taking to revise the agreement. Peel continued, stating that external parties have expressed the opinion that the current motion is inappropriate, and therefore he wishes to postpone the discussion. Secretary of State for War, Lord Hailsham, stated that the government is very grateful for Earl Peel's consideration. The government's reason for advocating postponement is that the developments in the Shanghai incident are not yet conclusive, and it cannot be determined whether discussing the matter would be beneficial to the public interest.

Guizhou Representative Discusses the Movement of the Guizhou Army and Chiang's Division

According to the East China News Agency, Jiang Zaizhen's division of the Guizhou Army has recently experienced sudden movements and has been surrounded by troops dispatched by Wang Jialie, the chairman of the province. A reporter from the East China News Agency yesterday interviewed Mr. Xu, a representative of the Guizhou provincial government, to inquire about the details. According to Xu, Jiang Zaizhen's division, currently stationed in Zunyi, has been recruiting bandits, intercepting tax revenues, and allowing its subordinates to extort money at will. Recently, it has also been spreading rumors to confuse public opinion. Furthermore, on the seventh day of this month, the division suddenly dispatched a regiment to deploy military forces on the north bank of the Wu River, cutting off transportation. Its elite troops, led by Yuan Binglin, also rushed to Yachi River and other places in Qianxi County to shell Song's troops stationed there, intending to occupy the counties of Qianxi and seize tax revenues, thereby cutting off Guiyang's economic lifeline. After receiving the report, Chairman Wang Jialie, considering that Jiang's troops were acting as rebels and undermining unity during this time of national crisis, convened a meeting of important generals in Guiyang. As a result of the discussion, they agreed to disarm Jiang Zaizhen's troops by force to prevent further chaos. On New Year's Day, they ordered Brigadier General Jian Wenbo to lead four regiments from Guiyang, and also ordered You Guocai's division stationed in Anshun and Che Mingyi's division stationed in Tongren to each dispatch two regiments to advance towards Zunyi in separate directions, forming an encirclement to resolve the issue of Jiang Zaizhen's troops. It is verified that although the division is nominally a division, it only has two infantry regiments. It is expected that the entire force can be subdued within ten days.

Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Statement on Telephone Rate Hike

The atmosphere of Shanghai citizens opposing the telephone rate hike had once subsided, but recently the Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association and the First District Citizens' Association are still working hard on this issue. In addition to sending letters to relevant local organizations, they have also sent telegrams to various ministries of the Nanjing government. Yesterday, the association received reply telegrams from the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and others. The telegram from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is as follows: "To the Shanghai Special District Citizens' United First District Branch and the Nanjing Road Business Community Association: Your telegram is acknowledged. If the matter of the Shanghai concession's telephone rate increase is as stated in your telegram, then the company's actions are indeed inappropriate and should be corrected to alleviate the burden on citizens. We have forwarded the situation to the Shanghai Municipal Government for investigation and handling. Sincerely, Ministry of Foreign Affairs."

The association also sent letters to the Chinese Ratepayers Association and the Municipal Council yesterday. The original texts are included below: (To the Chinese Ratepayers Association): "Respectfully, we have recently received reports from our members Sanxing Factory (telephone 94834), Hefeng (94944), Ren Changtai (94798), Maoshenghe (94717), Changfeng (94683), etc., stating that the telephone service of these companies has been disconnected by the Shanghai Telephone Company on November 13, either because they had already paid the original price for the autumn and winter quarters or because they were waiting for the resolution of the rate increase negotiations. We request that your association strive for a resolution. In this regard, our association, representing the majority of its members, believes that the massive price increase should not be imposed abruptly. We have listed our reasons and sent a letter to your association requesting you to strive for a reasonable resolution. Our association hopes that the company will cancel the compensation for the new price and set a fair price instead, which is a compromise that takes both sides into consideration. We originally hoped that the dispute would be resolved quickly. However, the company disregarded this intention and took unreasonable measures, claiming that it had obtained the approval of the Municipal Council, and therefore dared to oppress users and do whatever it wanted, regardless of everything. Furthermore, it has already accepted the old price. Cutting off the lines of users who have already paid for the autumn and winter quarters is even more of a fraudulent act and violates commercial ethics. If this situation continues, there will be no good outcome. If a fire breaks out in a disconnected user's premises during this period, and they suffer unlimited losses because they cannot use the telephone, resulting in an unsafe situation, who will be responsible? This matter concerns social security and public transportation. We are writing to you again, respectfully requesting your association to investigate and provide a swift remedy, expressing our friendship." (To the Municipal Council): "Respectfully, we have recently received reports from our members, the Shanghai Telephone Company's users Sanxing Factory (telephone 94834), Hefeng (94944), Ren Changtai (94798), Maoshenghe (94717), Changfeng (94683), etc., stating that the telephone service of these companies has been disconnected by the Shanghai Telephone Company on November 13, either because they had already paid the original price for the autumn and winter quarters or because they were waiting for the resolution of the rate increase negotiations. We request that your department strive for a resolution. In this regard, our association, representing the majority of its members, believes that the massive price increase should not be imposed abruptly. We have listed our reasons and sent a letter to your department requesting you to accommodate public opinion. Our association hopes that the company will cancel the compensation for the new price and set a fair price instead, which is a compromise that takes both sides into consideration. We originally hoped that the dispute would be resolved quickly. However, the company disregarded this intention and took unreasonable measures, claiming that it had obtained the approval of your bureau, and therefore dared to oppress users and do whatever it wanted, regardless of everything. Furthermore, it has already accepted the old price. Cutting off the lines of users who have already paid for the autumn and winter quarters is even more of a fraudulent act and violates commercial ethics. We fear that if this situation continues, there will be no good outcome. If a fire breaks out in a disconnected user's premises during this period, and they suffer unlimited losses because they cannot use the telephone, resulting in an unsafe situation, who will be responsible? We are writing to you again, requesting your bureau to accept the public opinion of the majority of Chinese citizens, and quickly approve the requests in our previous letter, ordering the Shanghai Telephone Company to set a new, fair price, and immediately stop the practice of disconnecting lines, in order to facilitate public transportation and maintain social security, expressing our sincere friendship."

Overseas Chinese Association Welcomes Huang Xu and Ji

The Overseas Chinese Association Held the Third Inaugural Meeting. On the evening of the 15th, the Overseas Chinese Association held a grand gathering at the R. Dong restaurant on Nanking Road to welcome the representatives of the overseas Chinese in Vietnam, Huang Xu and Ji. At the same time, a banquet was held, photographs were taken, and the third plenary meeting of the initiators was convened. At 7:00 p.m., the reception directors Fang Difei and Liang Shixiong were specially dispatched to the Dongya Hotel to receive the representatives Huang Xu and Ji. The presidium consisted of Guo Shun, Wu Chengyu, Zheng Juanian, Jian Yingfu, and Tang Haian. At 8:15 p.m., the meeting began. After respectfully reading the will of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the general secretary of the association, Peng Canguang, announced the reasons for the meeting (translated by Kong Gongwei). He briefly stated that the purpose of the association is to save the country and protect overseas Chinese, and it particularly focuses on movements to relieve the suffering of overseas Chinese. Just at the time of temporary preparation, the Vietnamese overseas Chinese representatives Huang and Ji, ignoring the long distance, returned to the country to petition for the Sino-French Commercial Treaty issue, hoping to relieve the suffering of hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese. The association expressed its deep sympathy and should adhere to the principle of mutual assistance, doing its best to assist the Vietnamese overseas Chinese in resolving their vital interests and completing the unfinished tasks of the representatives Huang and Ji. Therefore, tonight's meeting is not merely a welcoming formality, but a discussion on how to participate in and assist this practical work. Then, the chairman of the presidium, lawyer Wu Chengyu, delivered a welcome speech (the speech was lengthy and will not be reproduced in full). Representative Xu was then invited to report on the content of the Sino-French Commercial Treaty in Vietnam (omitted). Lawyer Wu Chengyu reported on assistance opinions (omitted). Speakers for free speeches included Cui Tongyue, Lai Yiren, and Master Yan Dajue. After the speeches, Representative Xu Yixian stood up to express his gratitude. The meeting adjourned at 5:20. Representatives Huang and Xu then left the meeting. The meeting was held at 9:30 p.m., with Wu Chengyu elected as the temporary chairman of the meeting and Hu Biaoyan as the recorder. Gao Qingyu reported on the matters (omitted). Five resolutions were made, including 1) The resolution on the second standing committee meeting of the preparatory committee and the resolution to assist Vietnamese overseas Chinese in resolving the Sino-French Commercial Treaty issue were approved. 2) Regarding the method of assisting Vietnamese overseas Chinese in resolving the Sino-French Commercial Treaty, it was resolved that the association would be given full power and the standing committee of the preparatory committee would be responsible for handling it, without the need to set up a separate organization. 3) Regarding the amendment of the name of the preparatory committee of the Overseas Chinese Association, deleting the word "temporary," the resolution was passed. 4) Regarding the addition of Jian Yingfu and Wu Chengyu as members of the preparatory committee presidium, the resolution was passed. 5) Regarding the continued solicitation of 1,000 initiators, the resolution was passed. 6) Regarding a certain case, the resolution was passed.

Yun Huifang's Appeal Case

Trial to Open on the 21st Afternoon. The appeal case of Yun Huifang has been scheduled to be heard on the afternoon of the 21st of this month at 1:00 PM at the Second Branch of the High Court. The grounds for appeal have also been drafted and will be submitted to the Second Branch of the High Court before being made public.

Suspecting Wife of Infidelity, Man Throws Infant to Death

Yu Longquan Listens to Friends' Rumors, Pitiful Girl Dies Wrongfully

Yu Longquan, the 25-year-old son of villager Yu Shenghe from No. 93, West Sanli Bridge, Pudong, is a plasterer. He married Zhao, who is 21 years old. They have been married for four years, but the relationship between the couple is very bad, and they often quarrel. This year, Zhao became pregnant. Yu Longquan heard rumors from his bad friend Ma Ligen, saying that Zhao had had an affair. Yu Longquan often argued that his wife's pregnancy was not his doing. Until last month, Zhao gave birth to a daughter. Yu Longquan was not at home. When he returned home the other day, he saw the child who was less than a month old and couldn't help but feel resentment. He immediately picked up the child and threw her to death. When he saw that the child was dead, he immediately fled. Yu Shenghe reported the news to the Third District, Third Precinct. In addition to detaining Yu Longquan for investigation, he ordered the local bailiff to report the case to the local court for examination yesterday.

Reasons for the Municipal Police Department's Detention of Military Equipment Samples

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Military Affairs previously learned of new military equipment recently invented in France. Therefore, it entrusted the Shanghai firm of Lihai & Co. to transport several samples of new anti-aircraft guns, machine guns, etc., to Nanjing for inspection. The ministry issued passes along the way as proof. Fu Xi, a Sichuan military officer, learned that the new military equipment was excellent and telegraphed the Shanghai firm of Xianghe & Co., requesting to transport it to Sichuan for inspection after the military inspected it. Therefore, the merchant shipped it from Nanjing to Sichuan the other day and loaded it on the Yongfeng Wheel the night before last to return to Shanghai. When it arrived in Shanghai, it was discovered by the special team of the Municipal Police Department that the number of pieces of military equipment did not match the number of pieces stated on the passport issued by the Ministry of Military Affairs. The military equipment was all detained. Yesterday, after learning of this, the merchant sent a representative to the Municipal Government to request its return. The negotiations are still in progress.

French Envoy Visits Mayor Wu

Mayor Wu Tiecheng of Shanghai, accompanied by Director of Education Pan Gongzhan and others, went to Hangzhou the other day and returned to Shanghai the night before last. Yesterday at around noon, French envoy Walle and Mr. Fessenden, Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, visited him successively and had lengthy discussions. It is reported that Mayor Wu is scheduled to visit them in return today.

Mayor Wu Hosts Banquet for League of Nations Health Commissioner

Mayor Wu hosted a banquet at his residence last night for Dr. Buzzi, a commissioner sent by the Health Section of the League of Nations to China. During the banquet, they also discussed the city's public health facilities.

Court Researching Case of Sealing Up Beixin Bookstore, Following Procedures

Has Not Yet Notified the Police, Not Refusal to Execute. A newspaper reported yesterday that the police refused to seal up the Beixin Bookstore. According to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency, the court is definitely following legal procedures to handle the case, and it has only had a joint research discussion with the police department. There has been no notification to execute the sealing.

Yu Hongjun Speaks. According to Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, the Municipal Government has not received formal notification about the police refusing to seal up the Beixin Bookstore. He is not certain about the details, so the Municipal Government is not in a position to comment. This matter is being handled under orders from the Central Government, and everything is being done according to the Central Government's instructions. In his personal opinion, whether or not the Beixin Bookstore has insulted Islam and whether or not its content constitutes criminal defamation are the prerequisites for the case. He understands that the Islamic Association has also requested Director-General Fessenden of the Ding Municipal Council to seal the store. It is unknown whether or not he has accepted the request. In light of the book industry's petition to withdraw the order, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has submitted a letter of request. However, the Municipal Government has simply forwarded the letter to the Central Government.

Municipal Government Proclamation. The Shanghai Municipal Government also issued a proclamation stating: "Proclamation regarding the incident. The Executive Yuan orders that ethnic equality and freedom of religion are the basic political tenets of our nation. The National Government, based on these tenets, has always supported all ethnic groups and religions in the country and has spared no effort. The Islamic people are an important component of the Republic of China and have made outstanding contributions to the party and the country, and have always been loved and respected by the whole country. However, it has been found that Beixin Bookstore, Nanhua Literary Society, and others have distributed insulting and malicious words against Islam, which is extremely absurd. Although the incident is minor, there is deep concern that distant rumors will cause misunderstandings. It has been ordered that the responsible agencies be severely dealt with according to law, to serve as a warning. In the future, all publications must not contain any form of contempt for any religion. In addition to the Government enforcing the law, it is hoped that all parties will be aware of the need to love and respect others, to discard differences and seek common ground. At this time of national crisis, it is especially important to strengthen unity and avoid causing incidents over minor matters. Let us all strive together. This is hereby proclaimed for general knowledge."

Lu Feibo Discusses the Beixin Bookstore Case

Only Seeking to Handle According to the Law, Not Protecting Beixin

Yesterday afternoon, a reporter visited Mr. Lu Feibo to inquire about the dispute between Islam and Beixin. Mr. Lu received the reporter and was asked whether the Islamic side had responded after the advertisement was published. Mr. Lu replied that he did not initially know that the Islamic community had established the United Association of Shanghai Mosques to handle the Beixin case, with an office in the Zhejiang Road Mosque. It was not until he met a member of the Islamic community, Mr. Huang, that he learned about it. Therefore, he went to the office at 11:00 AM this morning and was received by the Imam of the mosque, Mr. Ha Junde. Mr. Ha was very kind and said that the matter concerned the entire Islamic community and that he personally could not make any claims. He requested that a formal letter be sent to the association for consideration. After a brief discussion, he happily took his leave. However, at 3:00 PM, just as he was about to send the letter, he suddenly received a notification from Mr. Ha asking him not to send the letter, presumably because the opinions of the Islamic community were not yet unified. Mr. Lu also said that the insulting words against Islam in Beixin's publications were indeed unbearable. Not only the Islamic community hated it, but also many people in the book industry believed that such publications were a disgrace to the publishing industry. Recently, many people have sent letters to the Book Industry Association, questioning this matter. However, the Book Industry Association has no power to ban it. Beixin's offense against Islam is indeed deserved. Those in the industry who understand the situation will definitely not want to protect it in the slightest. Therefore, Beixin appealed to the industry association for assistance at the beginning of the incident, but the association refused because Beixin was to blame for its own troubles and did not want to be involved. Now, because of the administrative punishment and the change in the law, the impact is unimaginable. At this point, he could no longer stand by and watch, so he published the advertisement, hoping to negotiate a remedy with the Islamic representatives. This move was not only for the benefit of the entire publishing industry but also for the legal protection of the people of the whole country. Once this precedent is set, everyone will be in danger. He did not have the slightest intention to protect Beixin, and he hoped that the Islamic community would understand this. As for the word "mediation" in the advertisement, it was only intended to contact the Islamic community for consultations on remedies. As for the three proposed plans, they were all temporary assumptions and not fixed conditions. The Islamic community could exchange opinions during the face-to-face meeting. In short, if the Beixin case is handled according to the law, the Book Industry Association will have no objection, regardless of the outcome being unfavorable to Beixin. However, to seal the store without legal procedures is something that not only people in the industry will disagree with. The reporter then asked if the police had refused to carry out the order, as reported in the newspaper. Mr. Lu replied that he did not know and stated that the book industry had not applied to the Municipal Council. This matter concerns national dignity, and the book industry will definitely not do such a thing. The reason why he wanted to contact the Islamic community was not only for the benefit of the future of the book industry, but also to preserve the national dignity and the dignity of Islam. The reporter then asked about the rumor that the book industry would go on strike to protest. Mr. Lu declared emphatically that there would be no such action.

Shanghai in Statistical Tables

The book "Shanghai in Statistical Tables," recently compiled by the Institute of Social Sciences of the Academia Sinica, contains various statistics about Shanghai, divided into major categories such as meteorology, land and buildings, population, health, education, transportation, industry, labor, commerce, society, and municipal administration, forming a total of 274 tables. The materials in each table mostly start from the earliest period up to 1930. For example, meteorology and trade contain figures for the past 60 years. Each table is accompanied by footnotes, which not only specify the source of the materials, but also provide simple explanations of the meaning of the titles, as well as clarifications on the examination and correction of the figures, in order to ensure accuracy and reliability. The entire book has now been printed and will soon be advertised in major newspapers and periodicals. Readers are advised to pay attention.

Far East Sawmill Workers on Strike Yesterday

Last month, the Far East Sawmill in Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai, successively dismissed 32 workers. The labor side repeatedly requested reinstatement without effect. The workers were deeply angered and declared a general strike yesterday morning, putting forward four demands: (1) All dismissed workers should be reinstated; (2) Wages should be increased by 10%; (3) Workers should not be dismissed without reason; (4) Working hours should be reduced. They stated that they would not resume work until these demands were met. Upon receiving the report, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs dispatched personnel to investigate.

Westerner Fined for Indiscriminate Shooting

The Continental Daily reports that Mr. Meek, an engineer from Butterfield & Swire, was fined $32.50 (equivalent to 40 shillings in British currency) by the British Police Court yesterday for recklessly firing a handgun in Longhua on Sunday evening, endangering the public. He was warned that it was extremely foolish to discharge firearms in Chinese territory and was given a lenient punishment with the hope that he would not repeat the offense in the future. According to details of the case, a policeman from the Public Safety Bureau testified in court yesterday that he and two other policemen were patrolling the road on Sunday evening when they suddenly heard several gunshots coming from the east. They investigated to the front of the cement factory, where they saw a crowd gathered. Upon inquiry, they learned that a Westerner had been shooting indiscriminately. They searched the vicinity but found nothing. About ten minutes later, the defendant drove by in a car. Bystanders identified him as the Westerner who had fired the gun, so he was taken to the Public Safety Bureau and handed over to the authorities in the International Settlement. When questioned, the defendant claimed that he was shooting at the ground and did not endanger the public. The judge imposed a lenient fine and released him with a warning.

Pudong Ferry Households

Request to Designate a Permanent Ferry Dock. Lu Baokui and others from the Pudong Lannidu Ferry Business Office submitted a document to the Shanghai Municipal Government stating: "Submitting a document because the ferry dock has been abolished, livelihoods have been cut off, please designate a permanent ferry dock to provide relief and pacify the people. We, Baokui and 37 other households, are ferry operators in Lannidu, Pudong, generation after generation, relying on it to make a living. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities converted the Dongchang Wharf into a ferry, although the municipal government stated that the original ferry service operated by Baokui and others would still be allowed to continue operating, and the central ferry would be between Dongmen Road and Dongchang Road, and the ferry service of Baokui and others would be between Jiangtian Wharf and Lannidu, different routes, each unrelated. Even if other ferry terminals are established in the future, it is planned to reserve space for them to use. The documents are all there, showing the utmost concern of the municipal government for maintaining the livelihood of the people. However, recently, rumors spread that as a result of negotiations between the Bureau of Public Utilities and Huatong Zhan and Hongsheng Wharf, there would be a four-zhang-wide area north and south for the expansion of Dongchang Wharf. The implementation of a single ferry has already been decided, but the original ferry dock in Lannidu will be abolished, affecting not only the inability of Baokui and others to use the ferry, but also the inconvenience of commercial transportation and loading and unloading of goods. This is not a good plan. If it is implemented, Baokui and others will have no place to stand, and it will not be in accordance with the original intention of the previous municipal government's repeated statements. After repeated consideration, in order to ensure the safety of the ferry, we request that the municipal government investigate and stipulate that the current Lannidu Wharf or other suitable locations far from the municipal ferry be used as a permanent ferry dock. We believe that the livelihoods of dozens of families of Baokui and others are all due to the relief efforts of the municipal government, and we still earnestly request continuous maintenance and a swift designation of a permanent ferry dock, so that in the midst of vigorous construction, the intention of benefiting the people will not be lost. We are extremely apprehensive and await orders."

Visit to the Construction of the City Center District

The Municipal Government Scheduled to Host the Central Government: The Municipal Government has scheduled to host reporters from local newspapers and people from all walks of life at 1:00 PM this Saturday (the 19th) to visit the new municipal government building and various new constructions in the city center district. The invitation cards are scheduled to be sent out today.

Tang Haian Returns to Shanghai from Hong Kong

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, went to Hong Kong for private affairs and has now completed them. He returned to Shanghai by ship from Hong Kong the day before yesterday and visited the Songs on Qiqi Road yesterday afternoon.

Fire Destroys Chicken Brothel

A chicken brothel opened by Wang Laoer at No. 203 Ningbo Road in the French Concession suddenly caught fire due to carelessness at 4:42 PM yesterday. The flames raged uncontrollably.

It quickly spread to four neighboring buildings at Nos. 199, 201, 203, and 205. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire, which was not put out until 6:22 PM. It is heard that the losses were considerable.

Wu Tiecheng Sends Condolences for Wang Xiaolai's Deceased Wife

The wife of Mr. Tu Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, passed away in Hangzhou the day before yesterday. Mayor Wu telegraphed to Hangzhou yesterday to express his condolences. The original telegram said: "To Mr. Wang Xiaolai of Hangzhou, I was shocked to hear of the passing of your wife. I can hardly express my grief. I send this telegram to express my condolences. Please take care. Wu Tiecheng." (Stamped)

The Public Works Department Sends a Letter of Thanks to the French Concession Fire Brigade

The French Concession Fire Brigade went to the scene to assist in extinguishing the fire at the Minhang Road warehouse on the 11th of this month, which was extremely effective. Mr. Zhong Si, Director General of the Public Works Department, recently sent a letter to Mr. Foley, Secretary of the French Concession Municipal Council, asking him to convey the thanks of the Public Works Department and the Public Concession Fire Brigade to the members of the brigade.

Meeting Record of the Women's Advocate for National Goods Association

Discussion of the Association's Premises: The Shanghai Women's Advocate for National Goods Association held a joint meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road on the 15th. More than ten people attended, including Ouyang Zhiwen, Pan Tang Guanyu, Cai Zhoujun, Wang Xiaoying, Chen Jingrong, and Shu Huizhen. After the formalities were completed, Chairman Pan Tang Guanyu reported, stating in brief, "After the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the members of various committees dispersed and there was a lack of responsible personnel, which hindered the association's affairs. Although the war has subsided, the movement to advocate national goods should not be relaxed for a day, especially in our women's circles. Advocating national goods is the most effective weapon to defend against insults and save the country. This is why the association is in urgent need of reorganization. Currently, the association's premises are temporarily borrowed from No. 542 Zhonghua Road, which is only a temporary accommodation and not a permanent location. It seems appropriate to find another permanent location, which would be more convenient for handling affairs." After the chairman's report, the translation case was discussed. (1) In the case of moving the association's premises, it was decided that each committee member would separately select a suitable location and submit it to the next meeting for discussion. (2) In the case of determining the date of the next joint meeting, it was decided that a joint meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members would be convened at 4:00 PM on the 22nd of this month. The meeting adjourned at over six o'clock.

Telephone Users' Meeting Record

The Telephone Users' Association held its ninth board meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Zhang, Chen, Hu Fengxiang, Zhou Fuzhang, Chen Binghui, Qiu Liangyu, Zhuang Zhihe, Sun Wenyi, Zhang Xianfang, Liu Zhongying and others attended. Hu Fengxiang chaired the meeting. First, the chairman reported on the disconnections experienced by various users. Then, the following matters were discussed: (1) The Shanghai Citizen's First District Branch presented a case introducing Chang Cangshan, who is responsible for publicizing medical work and requested permission to join the association. It was decided to reply with approval, requesting Mr. Chang to work hard in publicizing. (2) A letter from Chinese taxpayers in the Shanghai Concession opposed the increase in telephone charges and urged the Director-General of the Public Works Department to reconsider the Board of Directors' decision. It was decided to wait for the Board of Directors' reconsideration before reaching a solution. (3) A case on resolutely opposing the price increase and again recommending representatives for negotiation. It was decided to recommend Hu Fengxiang, Zhou Fuzhang, Zhuang Zhihe, Qu Zhenhua, and Sun Wenyi to negotiate with the Public Works Department. (4) A case on how to deal with illegal disconnections by the company. It was decided that, before negotiations are completed, they will firmly express their opposition to the end, willing to make sacrifices to achieve the final victory, and will respond to the various users who have been disconnected. (5) A case recommending representatives from the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association to participate. It was decided to reply with approval. (6) The case of illegally increasing prices and requesting that the Municipal Government quickly grant negotiations. It was decided to petition the Municipal Government to negotiate according to law, in order to alleviate the burden on the people. Other proposals were also discussed. The meeting adjourned at approximately 5:00 PM.

Bandit's Heinous Acts

After Selling His Daughter, He Still Sends a Letter Demanding Extortion: Ten-Year-Old Cantonese Girl, He Huixiang, of Beautiful Appearance; Both Parents Deceased; Relies on Her Brother, He Fu, for Sustenance; Resides at Number 642 of 642 North Sichuan Road; Around 4 PM on the 19th of Last Month, While Playing at the Back Door, She Was Abducted by a Fellow Villager, Huang Darong, to the Home of a Friend Named Li on Liaoyang Road for One Night; The Next Day, He Took Her Near the Racecourse on Jing'an Temple Road, Colluding with Cantonese Woman Ma Lushi to Take Her to the Home of Ms. Ma at Number 1200 Kunshan Road, Detaining Her for Two Days; Ms. Ma, Together with Ms. Ma, Went to the Home of Cantonese Woman Liao Wenying at Tongfu Lane, Julieda Road, French Concession, Claiming That the He Girl's Family Was Destitute and Her Parents Had Died Early, Making Life Difficult, and Requested Assistance; Ms. Liao Was Considering Buying an Adopted Daughter to Alleviate Loneliness, and Upon Seeing Huixiang's Delicate and Charming Appearance, She Was Pleased and Gave 180 Silver Dollars, Establishing a Contract with Ma Lushi Signing as a Guarantor for Adoption; Huixiang, Being Young and Ignorant, Saw Ms. Liao's Wealthy Home and That They Were Fellow Villagers, and Felt Secure; Ms. Ma Obtained the Money and Shared It with Huang Darong and Others for Their Own Use; He Huixiang's Brother, He Fu, After His Sister Disappeared, Entrusted Someone to Search Everywhere; Believing in the Fortune Teller Qingluan, His Wife, Ms. Guo, Reported the Situation to the Hongkou Police Station and Entrusted His Cousin, Huang Neng, to Search, But He Was Unable to Find Her, and He Longed for Her Day and Night; On the 14th of This Month, He Fu Suddenly Received an Anonymous Letter Stating That His Sister Huixiang Had Been Located and That a Ransom of 1,000 Yuan Was Required for Her Return; The Letter Included a Drawing of a Handgun, Expressing Threatening Intentions, and Proposed a Meeting Near the Jiangwan Racecourse the Day Before Yesterday, Otherwise, the He Girl Would Face Dire Consequences; He Fu Took the Letter to the Police Station, and Sergeant Feng Shuofu Was Dispatched, Accompanied by He Ning, to Investigate and Apprehend Huang Darong at the Appointed Time, Learning of Ms. Ma's Residence and Discovering That Huang Neng Was the Instigator of the Crime; After the Incident, He Moved to Another Location on the 27th of Last Month; Inspector Feng Subsequently Apprehended Ms. Ma and Huang Neng, and Ms. Ma Confessed Where Huixiang Had Been Sold; The Police Secretly Rescued the Girl, Bringing Her to the Police Station Together; Huixiang Was Reclaimed by Her Brother, He Fu; The Police Chief Ordered the Three Suspects, Huang Darong, etc., to Be Detained Separately; Yesterday Morning, They Were Sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court; Police Lawyer Zhang Tianyin Stated the Previous Events and Claimed That the Police Station Would Not Prosecute Cantonese Woman Liao Wenying Because She Paid for Huixiang to Be Adopted, and There Was a Contract, and She Would Appear in Court Today as a Witness; Defendant Huang Darong Confessed to the Police That He Received 40 Yuan, Huang Neng Received 40 Yuan, Ms. Ma Lushi Received 70 Yuan, and the Fugitive Named Li Received 30 Yuan; The Anonymous Letter and the Girl's Sales Contract Were Submitted for Examination, Requesting a Postponement; Huang Darong Was Also Involved in a Theft Case, and So On; Subsequently, the Victim, He Fu, and His Wife, Ms. Guo, Explained the Course of Events; According to Huixiang, Defendant Huang Darong Tricked Me into Going Shopping Together, Then We Went to Ms. Ma Lushi's House, Where Ms. Ma Took Me to Liao Wenying's Place, etc.; According to Ms. Liao's Testimony, At That Time, Defendant Ma Lushi Brought Huixiang, Claiming That the Girl's Family Was Too Impoverished to Support Her and Requested to Adopt Her as a Goddaughter, Guaranteeing That There Would Be No Disputes in the Future, and She Was Deceived; When Questioned, Huang Darong Confessed That He Enticed the Girl and Entrusted Ma Lushi to Sell Her for a Price; Huang Neng Confessed, I Did Not Know About This Matter, Huang Darong Is Falsely Accusing Me of Prevaricating; Ma Lushi Confessed That Huang Darong Handed Huixiang to Me, Saying That the Girl's Family Was Poor and Asked Me to Sell Her to Ms. Liao as a Goddaughter, Which Is True; Huang Darong, at the End of Last Month, Stole Two Rolls of Silk Worth 26 Yuan from the Central Jixiang Store at Number 35 Hankou Road, and the Stolen Goods Were Also Brought to the Court; The Store Representative Provided Proof and Claimed Them; Judge Zhao Linyu Ordered the Three Defendants, Huang, etc., to Be Detained Separately and Re-Examined;

Stealing Blank Checks, Forging Signatures, Exposing Fraud

Shen Bianfu Escapes Midway; Han Liben Files Criminal Charges

Shen Bianfu, a native of Shaoxing and an employee of the Shenghe Railway Automobile Transportation Company at Number 201 of Julie Road, secretly used the key to the silver box at midnight on the 19th of Last Month to steal three blank checks from the Shanghai Bank, stamped the company's seal, and forged the names of Manager Han Liben and Associate Manager Xi Zishen; Around 11 AM on a Weekend Morning, He Filled Out the Check with the Current Date for 500 Yuan and Went to the Bank to Withdraw Cash; The Bank Teller Noticed That the Signature Did Not Match and Stopped Payment; Subsequently, the Company Reported the Incident to the Huizi Police Station, Which Sent Detectives to Arrest Shen and Bring Him to the Police Station; His Confession Was Evasive; The Police Chief Ordered Han and Xi to Take Him Back to File a Complaint or Seek a Reconciliation; Unexpectedly, Shen Took Advantage of the Situation to Escape Midway and Fled Without a Trace; Despite Various Searches, He Was Nowhere to Be Found; Manager Han Liben Had No Choice But to Hire Attorney Ying Qing to File a Lawsuit with the First Special District Court, Charging Him with Theft Under Article 337 of the Criminal Law and Forgery Under Article 234; Yesterday Afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui Convened a Hearing at Liwu; Plaintiff's Representative, Attorney Lin, Stated the Previous Events; According to Han Liben's Report, The Stubs of the Three Checks Were Also Torn Off by Shen Bianfu, Making It Impossible to Recover Them; Their Numbers Are 34228 (15), (827), (828), etc.; When Questioned, the Defendant Was Absent, and No Attorney Appeared to Defend Him; According to the Report of Chinese Constable Number 1281, The Defendant's Address Is Unknown, Making It Impossible to Serve a Summons; Judge Liu Ordered a Rescheduled Hearing to Summon the Defendant to Court for Verification;

Three Tragic Deaths

Poisoning Yesterday Evening Around 8 PM, a Young Man, About 30 Years Old, Dressed in a Western Suit, Arrived at the Dazhonghua Hotel on Xizang Road and Checked into Room 222; He Signed the Registration Book as Luo Ziming, a Local, and Paid the Room Fee; After the Waiter Brought Tea and Water, He Immediately Closed the Door and Went to Bed; Until Around 12:30 PM Yesterday, He Had Not Been Seen Getting Up, So the Waiter Inquired as Usual About Whether He Was Still in the Room; However, After Knocking on the Door for a Long Time Without a Response, He Became Suspicious and Tried to Open the Door, Only to See His Face Pale and His Breath Weak; He Immediately Reported to the Room Manager, Who Notified the Relevant Police Station and Used a Fire Brigade Ambulance to Send Him to Renji Hospital for Treatment; After the Doctor Gave Him an Injection and Poured Medicine, It Was Ineffective, and He Died at 10:30 PM That Night; The Corpse Was Transferred by the Hospital to the Morgue for Examination;

Swallowing Opium Ms. Ye Wang, a 26-Year-Old Woman from Anhui, Rented a Room at Number 115 Dongpushi Road; Her Husband, Ye Wenbing, Was a Painter at Texaco; Around 8 AM Yesterday Morning, After Getting Up, They Had a Quarrel Due to Joking, Which Led to a Dispute; Her Husband, Wenbing, Slapped Her Once; After the Neighbors Came Out to Mediate, Wenbing Left for Work; However, Ms. Ye, Feeling Unjustly Humiliated and Extremely Depressed, Suddenly Had the Thought of Death and Secretly Swallowed Raw Opium; Before Long, the Poison Took Effect, and She Groaned Uncontrollably; People Noticed Something Was Wrong and Quickly Sent Her to Renji Hospital for Treatment, But It Was Ineffective, and She Died Around 8 PM in the Evening;

Death by Falling Down The Suzhou Class Yuantong Small Wheel of the Local Yuantong Company Returned to Shanghai from Suzhou, Pulling Another Wuxi Passenger Boat; Unexpectedly, During the Journey, a Passenger About 40 Years Old on the Passenger Boat Suddenly Died Inside the Cabin; Yesterday, After the Wheel Arrived at the Port, Staff Member Xin Lizhen Reported the Incident to the Water Patrol Police Station, Which Dispatched Constable Su Jinlong to Transfer the Corpse to the Rescue Bureau for Coffin Preparation and Storage, Awaiting Family Members to Claim It;

Huazhong Chemical Plant Manufactures and Sells Copper Polishing Grease The Copper Beds and All Copperware Furnishings in Our Homes Are All Splendidly Pleasing to the Eye, Exquisite, and Beautiful; We Credit the Copperware Factories and Plating and Polishing Plants for Their Fine Manufacturing, But the Raw Material, Copper Polishing Grease, Still Relies on Imports; Little Do We Know That This Daily Enjoyment of Oil Polishing Costs Hundreds of Thousands of Dollars Annually; Chemical Experts Zhou Zhaoji and Xia Yuren, Gentlemen, Realized This and Conducted In-Depth Research for Several Years; Now, They Have Successfully Experimented with the Same Efficacy as Foreign Products; Because They Can Fully Utilize Domestic Raw Materials for Manufacturing, They Have Achieved the Goal of Low Price and High Quality; The Roughness of White Copper and Iron Utensils Can Be Smoothed, Refined, and Made Bright and Dazzling by This Oil on the Machine Wheel; Zhou Xia, Gentlemen, and Li Rongbao and Wu Lanzhou, Gentlemen, Have Organized a Huazhong Chemical Plant and Set Up a Manufacturing Department in Zhabei for Large-Scale Manufacturing; The Office Is Next to Shenbao in Hankou Road; It Is Reported That There Are Agencies in Nanjing and Zhenjiang, and Hardware Stores in Suzhou, Hangzhou, Wuhan, and Other Places Are Welcome to Act as Distributors;

Report on the Study of the Shanghai Public Concession by Judge Feitang, Volume 4 (25) Definition of Improper Conduct (Clause 20)

Any Public Official Who Violates This Ordinance, or Violates All the Regulations Stipulated in Accordance With This Ordinance, or Has One of the Following Acts, Shall Be Deemed to Have Improper Conduct:

1. Resisting, Despising, or Deliberately Failing to Comply With Lawful Orders Issued by Those With the Authority to Issue Orders, or Expressing Resistance in Language or Conduct, or,

2. Neglecting or Being Negligent in Performing Tasks, or

3. For Reasons Under His Control, Being Unsuitable or Incompetent for His Existing Position, or

4. Undertaking Any Private Agency Position or Work Related to His Public Duties Without the Approval Stipulated in Clause 93, or

5. Publicly Criticizing the Administration of Any Part of the Federal Government, or the Administration of Any Part of Any Provincial Government, or the Administration of the Areas Under His Entrusted Rule, or

6. Joining Any Political Group or Actively Participating in Any Political Event, or

7. Attempting to Interfere With the Public Official's Position, Promotion, or Salary With Political or External Forces, But the Provisions of This Article Do Not Prohibit Any Public Official From Seeking Redress for Any Grievances He Has Suffered Through Congress, or

8. Acting Indecently, Improperly, or Inappropriately, Expressing Rudeness to Other Public Officials or Any Members of Society During the Handling of Public Affairs, or

9. Drinking Excessive Amounts of Narcotics or Drugs to the Point of Becoming Addicted

Young Master Kidnaps His Own Son

Yesterday, I Saw in the Newspaper That Huang Zhengqing, a Young Master From Jin Yuan Money Bank in Zhenjiang, Lost More Than 10,000 Gold in Gambling and Could Not Think of a Way Out; He Ordered His Wet Nurse to Hide His Two-Year-Old Son and Falsely Accused His Father of Being Kidnapped by Bandits; In the End, Because the Procedures Were Not Complete, the Matter Was Exposed;

Kidnapping Cases Have Been Quite Popular Lately, and There Are Even Those Who Kidnap Friends, Relatives, and Employers, But Kidnapping One's Own Son Is the First Time I Have Heard of It; Huang Zhengqing Lost a Huge Sum of Money Due to Gambling and Could Not Think of a Solution, So He Kidnapped His Own Son for Ransom to Defraud His Father of Money; This Directly Kidnaps His Son's Ticket, but Indirectly Kidnaps His Father's Ticket; He Commits Both Gambling and Banditry Crimes, Which Are Extremely Evil; Old Huang's Beard Is Rising;

Recently, People's Hearts Have Changed Greatly; Sons Can Kidnap Fathers, and Fathers Can Kidnap Sons; That Is, in Kidnapping Cases, the Patterns Have Been Innovated and Are Full of Wonders; In Fact, Kidnapping Is Just an Abstract Noun; All Kinds of Illegal Means Are Used to Force Others to Give Money, or to Use Power to Make People Subordinate Unreasonably and Unable to Resist; None of Them Are Behaviors of a Kidnapping Nature; However, the Kidnapping of Kidnappers Still Has Facts to Prove and the Law Can Punish, While the Kidnapping of Non-Kidnappers Is Truly Impossible to Control; I Can Only Recite the Words of a Few Old Seniors:

Art and Literature

An Elegy on the Investigation and Burial of Starved Corpses in Linxia

— Sun Choucheng

Yesterday, I received a letter from a friend in Gansu, accompanied by an elegy by Deng Deyi on the investigation and burial of starved corpses in Linxia. It is so tragic that I transcribe it below to inform the readers:

My village suffers from the scourge of war,

The common people are mostly scattered.

Repeated pacifications and rebellions,

Hunger and cold are not easily avoided.

Remaining lives are left in ditches,

Barely prolonging their lingering breaths.

I sigh for the families of eight,

Most are barefoot.

If only they have enough grain inside,

Why bother distinguishing beans from wheat?

If only good rain comes,

Why worry about the weather being parched?

They deeply receive the grace of the great government,

But resent Yao and Tan being shallow.

I come to aid the displaced and deceased,

My heart is long, but my strength is short.

Cold leftovers and residual soup,

Are difficult to distribute to each bowl.

Inspecting the people's pallid faces,

Empty stomachs rumble like a pulley.

Emaciated faces are yellow and scorched,

Limbs of the dead are severed.

Flies and maggots suck blood and fat,

Dogs and pigs gnaw at hair braids.

New ghosts cry and say,

When will the armor be washed?

Old ghosts murmur and sigh,

Whose talent will be displayed?

Wanting to preserve their lives,

They bitterly twist their lips and beards.

Alas, people displaced by turmoil,

Are like wandering, homeless dogs.

White bones pile up like mountains,

Memorial mounds seal the earth.

Moved by this, I compose a lament,

Tears flow secretly as the song is completed.

Science

Turning Old Cotton into New Cotton

— Yi Wei

When cotton batting is used in clothes or bedding for a year or two, and the cotton fibers have not changed, it can be turned into new cotton with slight processing. It is not only soft, light, and warm, but also has excellent elasticity for dyeing.

(1) Tear the old cotton batting into small pieces, loosen it with a cotton gin (manual labor is also acceptable), and spray it with clean water.

(2) First boil an appropriate amount of clean water in a pot. Add caustic soda and dissolve it. Then, take the sprayed old cotton, put it into the pot, and boil it for three hours before捞起(lao qi). (When the steam rushes out of the pot, do not get your face too close.) Place it on a press to squeeze out the dark water, put it in a bamboo basket, wash it clean with clean water, and squeeze it dry.

(3) Use two wooden buckets, A and B. Drill a small hole in the bottom edge of bucket B. On the inside of the hole, nail a layer of fine lead wire mesh. Plug the hole with a wooden stopper. Pour bleaching powder into bucket A, dissolve it with a small amount of clean water, add more water, and stir well. Cover it and let it sit for four hours, without letting the gas escape. Connect bucket B to the leaking hole of bucket A. Remove the wooden stopper from bucket A, allowing the clarified bleaching powder water to leak into bucket B. Then pour it into a vat, add clean water, and stir (use cold water in summer and hot water in winter). Put the washed cotton into the bleaching powder water and stir well. Cover it tightly (do not let the gas escape, to prevent ineffective bleaching), soak it for twelve hours, take it out, wash it clean, and squeeze it dry.

(4) Put sulfuric acid into a clean water vat to make dilute sulfuric acid water. Put the bleached cotton into it and expose it for two hours. Take it out, wash it clean, and squeeze it dry.

(5) Put edible salt and alum into a clean water vat. Put the washed and squeezed cotton into it and submerge it for one hour. Take it out, wash it clean, squeeze it dry, and dry it in the sun. Loosen it with a cotton gin, or manually, and it becomes superior white cotton, even better than new cotton.

Recipe:

Old cotton: 30 catties

Edible salt (ground into powder): 5 taels

Bleaching Powder: 3 catties and 4 taels

Caustic Soda: 4 and a half catties

Alums: 6 taels

Sulluric Acid: 1 catty and 1 tael

School Photography

The Mysterious Love Letter

— A Yang

At X Girls' School, letters must be reviewed by a review committee organized by each grade before being distributed to individuals. This greatly hinders those who have love letters to exchange. Some clever individuals employ various means of networking, lobbying, and entertaining to ensure their letters pass safely. Others take the opportunity to blackmail or even openly announce the contents of the letters, leading to frequent jokes.

Everyone knows that Ms. K has a lover, but no one has ever found a love letter from him. Although she receives letters with red and green envelopes bearing her name every week, their contents are only a few short sentences or a poem-like text. Outsiders cannot fathom the situation. Indeed, some irrelevant descriptions are often found between the lines, which surprises the reviewers. As a result, not only has Ms. K become the subject of mysterious suspicion, but the reviewers have also vowed to crack this strange case.

Page 19

, compelling the review committee members to dedicate themselves to this mystery.

Another date arrived. Among a pile of thought-provoking 件 (jian, documents), Ms. 女士 (nv shi)'s letter was discovered again, naturally focusing their attention on it. However, the review revealed that it was still similar to the previous two letters, only a poem-like text with disjointed sentences. The original letter was as follows:

The bright moon hangs serenely in the sky,

How clear and tranquil the heavens are!

Three or five stars twinkle and sway,

The time is already utterly quiet!

The French哑铃(ya ling) plays a melody of longing,

The nation's destiny is so full of misfortune!

A beautiful flower and full moon are no longer timely!

The garden is desolate and autumn grieves!

Waiting for 娜(na), the angel to descend,

Do you remember? Fine scenery and auspicious time.

As the saying goes, "Three cobblers are equal to one Zhuge Liang." With the undivided attention of all the reviewers, the secret was discovered. It turned out to be a mysterious love letter with a rendezvous, the sentences were barely pieced together, only the first character of each line was important, which was "Tomorrow at three, French Garden, waiting for you." With the truth revealed, everyone felt the novelty of the matter and admired Ms. K's lover's ingenuity. Instantly, the news spread throughout the school, and Ms. K blushed, surrounded by her classmates' laughter.

Behind the Scenes

New Methods of Extortion

— Li Huo

Zhang Jun, whom I hadn't seen for a long time, suddenly arrived at my humble abode yesterday, causing me unexpected joy. I hurriedly invited him into the house to discuss his current situation after our long separation. After some pleasantries, I learned from his conversation that Zhang Jun had recently opened a store in Hongkou, and the business was not bad. He also told me about a recent extortion incident, which I record here for the benefit of others.

Yesterday afternoon, I (Zhang Jun himself) came out of a relative's house and planned to take the No. 6 tram back to the store. As I was lingering at the tram stop, a young man suddenly appeared in my sight. He opened his mouth and said:

"Brother Zhang, how have you been lately? Where are you making a fortune? Brother has been in dire straits recently, to tell you the truth, so poor that I can't even afford three meals a day. I heard that you have been very successful recently, and your residence has recently been rented on Haining Road. Brother should have come to visit, but I am ashamed of my tattered clothes. It is fortunate that we met today. Last year, when you were in the village, you borrowed ten yuan from me, which has not been returned to this day. I suppose you have forgotten it because you are a busy person. Brother should not be so presumptuous as to urge you to repay this small sum, but because I am drifting at sea and have no means of income and no relatives to rely on, I have no choice but to shamelessly beg you. I hope my brother will not blame me!"

I was so confused by his flowery words that I couldn't make heads or tails of it. I had never met such a person before. When I tried to argue that he was mistaken, he insisted that we had gone to school together since childhood and that he was a relative. His surname was Wang, and his sister-in-law's aunt and my mother were blood sisters. In May of last year, I had asked him to buy ten yuan worth of clothing material in Shanghai. We used to visit each other often, but now that I am poor, I don't even recognize my friends anymore. Gentlemen, what kind of logic is that! Many bystanders felt that his reasons were sufficient and even produced my resume, mocking me for not treating my friends like that.

At that time, he was scolding me for no reason in front of everyone. Relying on his eloquence, he made me blush and left me speechless, with no room for argument. Later, someone came out to mediate and told me to give him one yuan to settle the matter. At that time, I was in a dilemma, so I had to admit my bad luck and gave him one yuan to get rid of him. After I inquired, I found out that there are indeed such rogues who specialize in extorting money from passengers at tram stations and transportation hubs. Those who are extorted have no way to argue. They specialize in inquiring about people's resumes. Once they find out, they can start their business. Those who are good at it can cheat more than a hundred yuan at a time. However, they also size up their victims. They would never patronize those who are old Shanghai residents. I advise all honest comrades not to fall into their trap.

One Scale, One Claw

A New Interpretation of Code Words

— Yun Zong

The Japanese imperialists are engaging in militarism, invading our territory, slaughtering our people, plundering our wealth, disregarding humanity, and ignoring justice, acting wantonly. They are truly 虧對頭寡婦 (kui dui tou gua fu) – losing out against the widow (unlawful and reckless)! "法 (fa, law)" is a mispronunciation of "髮 (fa, hair)."

During the Battle of Shanghai, the 19th Route Army resisted the Japanese to the death, repeatedly thwarting the enemy's advance. The world was shocked and admired their bravery. They are truly 高山上敲鑼 (gao shan shang qiao luo) – hitting a gong on a high mountain (famous in all directions)! "名 (ming, name)" is a homophone of "鳴 (ming, sound)."

Important figures in the Party, at a time when internal and external troubles are pressing, are still either visiting famous mountains and scenic spots or indulging in fine wine and beautiful women. They are truly 肉骨頭敲鼓 (rou gu tou qiao gu) – beating a drum with a meaty bone (昏𥋾𥋾 (hun dong dong) – muddled)! "葷鼕鼕 (hun dong dong)" is a homophone.

The nation is in dire straits, yet some military men and politicians still fight for power and profit, acting like overlords. They are truly 買了乾魚放生 (mai le gan yu fang sheng) – buying dried fish and releasing it (弗得知死活 (fu de zhi si huo) – not knowing whether to live or die)!

The armed class commits crimes and evils, but the government cannot punish them according to the law. They are truly 張天師被鬼迷 (zhang tian shi bei gui mi) – Zhang Tianshi being bewitched by a ghost (有法没用 (you fa mei yong) – having the law but not using it)!

Treacherous merchants sell enemy goods, only wanting to make money for themselves, regardless of whether the nation is doomed. They are truly 棺材裏伸手 (guan cai li shen shou) – reaching out from the coffin (死要錢 (si yao qian) – desperately wanting money)!

Casual Chat

Shifting Thoughts

— Kang Shi

I. Random Notes

We seek money to survive, but are seduced and bewildered by its power, causing us to fall and fail, ultimately losing our ability to survive.

The more civilized a place is in terms of material wealth and the more advanced it is in terms of scholarship, the more rampant evil grows. If you don't believe me, take a look at Shanghai! Adultery, theft, and murder fill the newspapers every day!

Everyone says that we should cast off hypocrisy in life, but life is ultimately inseparable from it. The greater the person, the greater the hypocrisy... Where is there a word of truth?

Venereal disease doctors seem to be practicing medicine to save the world and ferrying people across the sea of suffering, but in reality, something seems amiss. Because many people hold the preconceived notion of being prepared for any eventuality, the more venereal disease doctors there are, the more people suffer from venereal diseases.

II. What is Meant by Jointly Meeting the National Crisis?

A: What is meant by jointly meeting the national crisis?

B: It means jointly saving the nation from its crisis.

A: No, no, jointly meeting means jointly promoting. Promoting means accelerating. It means jointly accelerating the national crisis. Don't you see that several civil wars have broken out during this time of national crisis? Isn't that jointly accelerating the national crisis?

B: Yes, yes.

III. Two Radically Different Faces

When the manager speaks to the clerk, his face is very stern. At the same time, the clerk's face has no choice but to wear a pleasant expression. Radically different!

When the police officer raises his baton to hit the rickshaw puller, his face is very fierce. At the same time, the rickshaw puller's face is very frightened! Pitiful! Radically different!

When a beggar asks for money, his face is very sad. At the same time, the face he turns away has a very disgusted and angry expression. Radically different!

IV. The Most Patriotic People are Villagers

A friend said, "The most patriotic people are villagers."

I said, "How do you know?"

He replied, "Villagers' clothing, food, and shelter are all made of domestic goods! Whereas in the cities, the clothing, food, and shelter are mostly imported!"

Short Story

Humanity

— Wu

The humanitarian was sitting in a rickshaw. When he passed the Bund, he saw many coolies with disheveled hair and dirty faces painfully hauling goods with all their might, groaning and moaning. He felt very sad, and he couldn't help but feel heartbroken:

"Ah! This is simply a living hell, it is truly inhuman. But why do these coolies have to do this? Can't they find other jobs? Since they are human beings, why do they have to live like cattle and horses? Alas! They are truly a bunch of stupid pigs!" So his noble compassion inevitably turned to disdain for them. But then he thought, "But they are very pitiful after all, they can't eat their fill, they can't keep warm, everyone should sympathize with them. That's right, I should pity them, I can give them some copper coins, they will definitely be very grateful. Moreover, this is a very good opportunity for me to accumulate good karma. By doing this, my morality will certainly be elevated a lot.

So he displayed great compassion, and his tender, plump white hand reached into his pocket and took out a handful of copper coins, which he threw down from the rickshaw with a clatter. Of course, this group of hungry people would madly rush forward to pick up the coins. Those who picked them up wanted to pick up more, and those who didn't pick them up wanted to pick them up even more. Each copper coin was like their own life, fighting and grabbing, resulting in him snatching it from his hand, and him snatching it back from his hand. So they cursed, beat each other, rolled on the ground, and twisted around the wheels of the car. Some people even stepped over them, and soon their faces were covered in blood. At this time, the humanitarian felt very honored, "Oh, I have done a good deed." He couldn't help but jump out of the rickshaw, stick out his chest, walk forward, and shout in a loud voice: "Don't fight, why do you have to fight? I'll give you a few more."

Another clatter, another group of people rushed from all directions, again grabbing and snatching. Indeed, they were doing it for survival, for hunger, why shouldn't they do it?

Of course, our humanitarian felt even more "good karma," and a feeling of happiness welled up from his heart, followed by a burst of laughter. But he immediately encountered two angry gazes sweeping across his face, followed by a big man pointing at him and roaring:

"Are you laughing at us? Are you laughing at us fighting? Are you giving us a few copper coins to teach us to fight for you? Bastard!"

"Hey! I am kindly helping you, do you have to offend me?" he said resentfully. "They are truly a group of beasts who don't know gratitude!"

"Oh? You are helping us?" Another person said, "Thank you for your kindness, but why are you laughing at us as we fight for your few copper coins and our faces are covered in blood? Isn't this intentionally making fun of us?"

The crowd shouted loudly, making him feel fearful. So he immediately shrank his body and fled, quickly jumping back into the original rickshaw, shouting to the driver, "Quick! Quick! Go!"

In front of him, he encountered an armed policeman, so he hurriedly asked the policeman to quickly suppress the situation, on the grounds that a group of "cattle and horses" were shouting and trying to beat him.

The policeman also seemed to take it seriously and hurriedly ran over.

He didn't breathe a sigh of relief until he reached his own door. He saw that the rickshaw puller was covered in sweat.

After a while, the rickshaw puller took the money and asked for a few more coins, but he did not allow it, saying:

"Didn't I agree with you on two dimes? What are you arguing about?"

"No, sir! I ran too fast, I'm too tired, and I waited for you for so long on the Bund."

"Don't worry about that, not another dime."

"But please, sir, do a good deed, we are too pitiful!"

But this humanitarian finally slammed the door shut with a bang, resentfully.
